--- File: src/components/assistant/AssistantConsoleClient.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select";
import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import { getQueueStatus, callNextTicket, recallLastCalledTicket } from '@/actions/queueActions';
import type { QueueState, Ticket } from '@/types/queue';
import type { SessionUser } from '@/types/user';
import { LoadingSpinner } from '@/components/common/LoadingSpinner';
import { BellRing, ListChecks, RefreshCw, Tv2, UserPlus, Home, Settings, User, HeartHandshake, Wrench } from 'lucide-react';
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import Link from 'next/link';
import { Badge } from '../ui/badge';

export function AssistantConsoleClient({ initialQueueState, currentUser }: { initialQueueState: QueueState, currentUser: SessionUser }) {
  const [queueState, setQueueState] = useState<QueueState>(initialQueueState);
  const [isLoadingGlobal, setIsLoadingGlobal] = useState(false);
  const [isCallingNext, setIsCallingNext] = useState(false);
  const [isRecalling, setIsRecalling] = useState(false);
  const [selectedWindow, setSelectedWindow] = useState<number | undefined>(undefined);
  const { toast } = useToast();

  const canAccessSettings = currentUser.role === 'admin' || currentUser.role === 'superadmin';
  const canAccessTools = canAccessSettings || currentUser.role === 'supervisor';

  const fetchAndUpdateState = useCallback(async (isUserInitiatedAction = false) => {
    if (isUserInitiatedAction) setIsLoadingGlobal(true);
    try {
      const newState = await getQueueStatus();
      setQueueState(newState);
      if (isUserInitiatedAction) {
        toast({ title: "Estado Actualizado", description: `Sincronizado a la versión ${newState._version} de la cola.` });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching state:", error);
      if (isUserInitiatedAction) {
        toast({ title: "Error de Sincronización", description: "No se pudo obtener el estado más reciente de la cola.", variant: "destructive" });
      }
    } finally {
      if (isUserInitiatedAction) setIsLoadingGlobal(false);
    }
  }, [toast]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchAndUpdateState(false); // Initial fetch on mount
    const intervalId = setInterval(() => fetchAndUpdateState(false), 7000); // Poll every 7 seconds
    return () => clearInterval(intervalId);
  }, [fetchAndUpdateState]);

  useEffect(() => {
      if (queueState.operationMode === 'multi' && queueState.availableWindows.length > 0) {
        if (!selectedWindow || !queueState.availableWindows.includes(selectedWindow)) {
          setSelectedWindow(queueState.availableWindows[0]);
        }
      } else {
        setSelectedWindow(undefined);
      }
  }, [queueState.availableWindows, queueState.operationMode, selectedWindow]);

  const playCallSound = () => {
    try {
        const audio = new Audio('/sounds/call-sound.mp3');
        audio.play().catch(error => {
            console.warn("Error al reproducir sonido (puede ocurrir antes de la interacción del usuario):", error);
        });
    } catch(e) {
        console.error("No se pudo reproducir el sonido de llamada:", e);
    }
  };

  const handleCallNext = async () => {
    setIsCallingNext(true);
    try {
      const params = queueState.operationMode === 'multi' ? { windowNumber: selectedWindow } : {};
      if (queueState.operationMode === 'multi' && queueState.availableWindows.length > 0 && !selectedWindow) {
        toast({ title: "Puesto Requerido", description: "Por favor seleccione un puesto de atención.", variant: "destructive" });
        setIsCallingNext(false);
        return;
      }
      const result = await callNextTicket(params);
      if (result.success && result.updatedState) {
        setQueueState(result.updatedState);
        if (result.calledTicket) {
          playCallSound();
          toast({ title: "Ticket Llamado", description: `Ticket ${result.calledTicket.displayNumber} ${result.calledTicket.window ? `a puesto ${result.calledTicket.window}` : ''} llamado.` });
        } else {
          toast({ title: "Información", description: result.message || "No hay tickets para llamar o acción no completada.", variant: "default" });
        }
      } else {
        toast({ title: "Error al llamar", description: result.message || "No se pudo llamar al siguiente ticket.", variant: "destructive" });
        if (result.updatedState) setQueueState(result.updatedState); else await fetchAndUpdateState();
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast({ title: "Error de Sistema", description: "Ocurrió un error de comunicación.", variant: "destructive" });
      await fetchAndUpdateState();
    } finally {
      setIsCallingNext(false);
    }
  };
  
  const handleRecallTicket = async () => {
    setIsRecalling(true);
    try {
      const params = queueState.operationMode === 'multi' ? { windowNumber: selectedWindow } : {};
      if (queueState.operationMode === 'multi' && queueState.availableWindows.length > 0 && !selectedWindow) {
        toast({ title: "Puesto Requerido", description: "Por favor seleccione un puesto para volver a llamar.", variant: "destructive" });
        setIsRecalling(false);
        return;
      }
      const result = await recallLastCalledTicket(params);
      if (result.success && result.updatedState) {
        setQueueState(result.updatedState);
        if (result.recalledTicket) {
          playCallSound();
          toast({ title: "Ticket Re-Llamado", description: `Ticket ${result.recalledTicket.displayNumber} ${result.recalledTicket.window ? `a puesto ${result.recalledTicket.window}` : ''} vuelto a llamar.` });
        } else {
          toast({ title: "Información", description: result.message || "No se pudo volver a llamar el ticket.", variant: "default" });
        }
      } else {
        toast({ title: "Error al re-llamar", description: result.message || "No se pudo volver a llamar el ticket.", variant: "destructive" });
        if (result.updatedState) setQueueState(result.updatedState); else await fetchAndUpdateState();
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast({ title: "Error de Sistema", description: "Ocurrió un error de comunicación.", variant: "destructive" });
      await fetchAndUpdateState();
    } finally {
      setIsRecalling(false);
    }
  };

  const handleUserInitiatedRefresh = async () => {
    await fetchAndUpdateState(true);
  };

  const waitingGeneralCount = queueState.tickets.filter(t => t.status === 'waiting' && t.type === 'general').length;
  const waitingPreferentialCount = queueState.tickets.filter(t => t.status === 'waiting' && t.type === 'preferential').length;
  const waitingTicketsCount = waitingGeneralCount + waitingPreferentialCount;
  
  const nextGeneralTicket = queueState.tickets.find(t => t.status === 'waiting' && t.type === 'general');
  const nextPreferentialTicket = queueState.tickets.find(t => t.status === 'waiting' && t.type === 'preferential');

  const canCallNext = queueState.manualDispenserMode || waitingTicketsCount > 0;
  const callButtonDisabled = isCallingNext || isLoadingGlobal || isRecalling || !canCallNext ||
    (queueState.operationMode === 'multi' && queueState.availableWindows.length === 0) ||
    (queueState.operationMode === 'multi' && !selectedWindow);

  const canRecall =
    (queueState.operationMode === 'single' && !!queueState.nowServing) ||
    (queueState.operationMode === 'multi' && !!selectedWindow && !!queueState.activeWindows[selectedWindow]);

  const recallButtonDisabled = isRecalling || isCallingNext || isLoadingGlobal || !canRecall;


  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-background to-secondary/30">
      <div className="container mx-auto p-4 md:p-8 flex-grow">
        <header className="mb-8 flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-center gap-4">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <BellRing className="h-10 w-10 text-primary" />
            <h1 className="text-4xl font-bold tracking-tight">Consola de Operador</h1>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap justify-center sm:justify-end">
            <Button variant="outline" onClick={handleUserInitiatedRefresh} disabled={isLoadingGlobal || isCallingNext || isRecalling}>
                <RefreshCw className={`mr-2 h-4 w-4 ${isLoadingGlobal ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
                Refrescar
            </Button>
            <Link href="/kiosk" passHref legacyBehavior><Button variant="outline" asChild><a><UserPlus className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Ir a Kiosko</a></Button></Link>
            <Link href="/display" passHref legacyBehavior><Button variant="outline" asChild><a><Tv2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Ver Pantalla</a></Button></Link>
            {canAccessTools && <Link href="/tools" passHref legacyBehavior><Button variant="outline" asChild><a><Wrench className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Herramientas</a></Button></Link>}
            {canAccessSettings && <Link href="/settings" passHref legacyBehavior><Button variant="outline" asChild><a><Settings className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Configuración</a></Button></Link>}
            <Link href="/" passHref legacyBehavior><Button variant="outline" asChild><a><Home className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Menú Principal</a></Button></Link>
          </div>
        </header>

        <Card className="shadow-lg rounded-xl bg-card max-w-4xl mx-auto">
            <CardHeader>
              <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-2xl"><ListChecks /> Estado de la Cola</CardTitle>
              <CardDescription>Gestione los turnos y llame a los siguientes clientes.</CardDescription>
            </CardHeader>
            <CardContent className="space-y-6">
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6 items-start">
                <div className="space-y-4">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-around p-4 bg-secondary/50 rounded-lg">
                        <div className='text-center'>
                          <p className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1.5"><User className='h-4 w-4'/> General</p>
                          <p className="text-3xl font-bold">{waitingGeneralCount}</p>
                          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Siguiente: {nextGeneralTicket?.displayNumber ?? '-'}</p>
                        </div>
                        <div className='text-center'>
                          <p className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1.5"><HeartHandshake className='h-4 w-4'/> Preferencial</p>
                          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-blue-600">{waitingPreferentialCount}</p>
                          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Siguiente: {nextPreferentialTicket?.displayNumber ?? '-'}</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                     {queueState.operationMode === 'multi' && queueState.availableWindows.length > 0 && (
                        <div className="space-y-2">
                          <Label htmlFor="window-select">Seleccionar Puesto de Llamada</Label>
                          <Select value={selectedWindow?.toString()} onValueChange={(val) => setSelectedWindow(Number(val))} disabled={isLoadingGlobal || isCallingNext || isRecalling} >
                              <SelectTrigger id="window-select" className="w-full">
                                <SelectValue placeholder="Seleccione puesto" />
                              </SelectTrigger>
                              <SelectContent>
                              {queueState.availableWindows.map(winNum => (
                                <SelectItem key={winNum} value={winNum.toString()}>
                                  <span className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                                    Puesto {winNum}
                                    {queueState.preferentialWindows.includes(winNum) && <Badge variant="outline" className='bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 border-blue-300'>Pref.</Badge>}
                                  </span>
                                </SelectItem>
                              ))}
                              </SelectContent>
                          </Select>
                        </div>
                    )}
                </div>

                <div className="space-y-3">
                    <Button onClick={handleCallNext} className="w-full h-16 text-xl bg-accent text-accent-foreground hover:bg-accent/90" disabled={callButtonDisabled} >
                    {isCallingNext ? <LoadingSpinner /> : "Llamar Siguiente"}
                    </Button>
                    <Button
                        onClick={handleRecallTicket}
                        className="w-full"
                        variant="outline"
                        disabled={recallButtonDisabled}
                    >
                        {isRecalling ? <LoadingSpinner /> : <> Volver a Llamar Último</>}
                    </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
             
              <Separator />

              <div className="mt-4">
                <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Atendiendo Actualmente:</h3>
                {queueState.operationMode === 'single' && queueState.nowServing && (
                  <div className="text-xl p-3 bg-primary/10 dark:bg-primary/20 rounded-md flex justify-between items-center">
                    <span>Ticket <span className="font-bold text-primary">{queueState.nowServing.displayNumber}</span></span>
                    {queueState.nowServing.type === 'preferential' && <Badge className='bg-blue-500 text-white'>Preferencial</Badge>}
                  </div>
                )}
                {queueState.operationMode === 'multi' && (
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 md:grid-cols-4 gap-2">
                    {queueState.availableWindows.map(winNum => {
                      const ticket = queueState.activeWindows[winNum];
                      return (
                        <div key={winNum} className="p-3 border rounded-md">
                          <div className='flex justify-between items-center mb-1'>
                            <span className="font-semibold">Puesto {winNum}:</span>
                            {queueState.preferentialWindows.includes(winNum) && <Badge variant="outline" size="sm" className='text-xs bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 border-blue-300'>Pref.</Badge>}
                          </div>
                          {ticket ? (
                            <div className='flex justify-between items-center'>
                              <span className="text-primary font-bold">{`T-${ticket.displayNumber}`}</span>
                              {ticket.type === 'preferential' && <HeartHandshake className='h-4 w-4 text-blue-500'/>}
                            </div>
                          ) : (
                            <span className="ml-2 text-muted-foreground">Libre</span>
                          )}
                        </div>
                      );
                    })}
                    {queueState.availableWindows.length === 0 && <p className="text-muted-foreground col-span-full text-center">No hay puestos activos. Vaya a Configuración para añadirlos.</p>}
                  </div>
                )}
                {queueState.operationMode === 'single' && !queueState.nowServing && ( <p className="text-muted-foreground">Esperando para llamar...</p> )}
              </div>
              <p className="text-xs text-center mt-4 text-muted-foreground">
                Cola v{queueState._version}
              </p>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
      </div>
      <footer className="w-full text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground py-8">
        <p>&copy; {new Date().getFullYear()} Clic Soporte & Clic Tienda S.R.L. Todos los derechos reservados.</p>
        <p className='font-mono text-xs mt-1'>{queueState._version}</p>
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

--- File: src/components/auth/ActivationForm.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState } from 'react';
import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
import * as z from 'zod';
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Form, FormControl, FormField, FormItem, FormLabel, FormMessage } from '@/components/ui/form';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useToast } from '@/hooks/use-toast';
import { KeyRound, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { activateLicense, useFreeVersion } from '@/actions/licenseActions';
import type { LicenseState } from '@/types/license';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { Separator } from '../ui/separator';

const formSchema = z.object({
  licenseKey: z.string().min(1, { message: 'La clave de licencia es requerida.' }),
});

type FormValues = z.infer<typeof formSchema>;

export function ActivationForm({ initialLicenseState }: { initialLicenseState: LicenseState }) {
    const { toast } = useToast();
    const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
    const [licenseState, setLicenseState] = useState<LicenseState>(initialLicenseState);

    const form = useForm<FormValues>({
        resolver: zodResolver(formSchema),
        defaultValues: {
            licenseKey: '',
        },
    });

    const onSubmit = async (values: FormValues) => {
        setIsLoading(true);
        try {
            const result = await activateLicense(values.licenseKey);
            setLicenseState(result);
            if (result.isValid) {
                toast({
                    title: 'Activación Exitosa',
                    description: 'La licencia ha sido activada correctamente. La aplicación se recargará.',
                });
                setTimeout(() => window.location.reload(), 2000);
            } else {
                toast({
                    title: 'Error de Activación',
                    description: result.message || 'La clave de licencia no es válida o no se pudo activar.',
                    variant: 'destructive',
                });
            }
        } catch (error) {
             toast({
                title: 'Error de Sistema',
                description: 'No se pudo comunicar con el servidor de licencias.',
                variant: 'destructive',
            });
        } finally {
            setIsLoading(false);
        }
    };
    
    const handleUseFreeVersion = async () => {
        setIsLoading(true);
        try {
            const result = await useFreeVersion();
            if (result.success) {
                toast({
                    title: 'Versión Gratuita Activada',
                    description: 'La aplicación se ejecutará en modo gratuito. Recargando...',
                });
                setTimeout(() => window.location.reload(), 2000);
            } else {
                toast({
                    title: 'Error',
                    description: result.message,
                    variant: 'destructive',
                });
            }
        } catch (error) {
            toast({
                title: 'Error de Sistema',
                description: 'No se pudo cambiar al modo gratuito.',
                variant: 'destructive',
            });
        } finally {
            setIsLoading(false);
        }
    };


  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-4 bg-gradient-to-br from-background to-secondary/30">
      <Card className="w-full max-w-md shadow-2xl">
        <CardHeader className="text-center">
            <div className="mx-auto mb-4">
               <KeyRound className="h-16 w-16 text-primary" />
            </div>
            <CardTitle className="text-3xl font-bold">Activación Requerida</CardTitle>
            <CardDescription>
                Por favor, ingrese su clave de licencia para activar el sistema.
            </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
            <Form {...form}>
                <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="space-y-6">
                    <FormField
                        control={form.control}
                        name="licenseKey"
                        render={({ field }) => (
                            <FormItem>
                                <FormLabel>Clave de Licencia</FormLabel>
                                <FormControl>
                                    <Input placeholder="XXXX-XXXX-XXXX-XXXX" {...field} />
                                </FormControl>
                                <FormMessage />
                            </FormItem>
                        )}
                    />
                    {licenseState.message && (
                        <p className={cn("text-sm text-center", licenseState.isValid ? "text-green-600" : "text-destructive")}>
                           {licenseState.message}
                        </p>
                    )}
                    <Button type="submit" className="w-full" disabled={isLoading}>
                        {isLoading && <Loader2 className="mr-2 animate-spin" />}
                        Activar Sistema
                    </Button>
                </form>
            </Form>
             <Separator className="my-6" />
             <div className="text-center">
                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-4">O si no tiene una licencia:</p>
                <Button variant="outline" className="w-full" onClick={handleUseFreeVersion} disabled={isLoading}>
                    {isLoading && <Loader2 className="mr-2 animate-spin" />}
                    Continuar con la versión gratis
                </Button>
             </div>
             <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-6 text-center">
                <p>Hardware ID: <span className="font-mono">{licenseState.hardwareId}</span></p>
             </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
       <footer className="mt-8 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            <p>&copy; {new Date().getFullYear()} Clic Soporte & Clic Tienda S.R.L.</p>
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

"use client";

import { useState } from 'react';
import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
import * as z from 'zod';
import { createFirstUser } from '@/actions/userActions';
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Form, FormControl, FormField, FormItem, FormLabel, FormMessage } from '@/components/ui/form';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useToast } from '@/hooks/use-toast';
import { UserPlus } from 'lucide-react';
import { LoadingSpinner } from '../common/LoadingSpinner';

const formSchema = z.object({
  username: z.string().min(3, { message: 'El usuario debe tener al menos 3 caracteres.' }),
  password: z.string().min(6, { message: 'La contraseña debe tener al menos 6 caracteres.' }),
  companyName: z.string().min(2, { message: 'El nombre de la empresa es requerido.' }),
});

type FormValues = z.infer<typeof formSchema>;

export function CreateFirstUserForm() {
    const { toast } = useToast();
    const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

    const form = useForm<FormValues>({
        resolver: zodResolver(formSchema),
        defaultValues: {
            username: 'admin',
            password: '',
            companyName: 'Clic Tienda Turnos',
        },
    });

    const onSubmit = async (values: FormValues) => {
        setIsLoading(true);
        try {
            const result = await createFirstUser(values.username, values.password, values.companyName);
            if (result.success) {
                toast({
                    title: '¡Administrador Creado!',
                    description: 'El primer usuario administrador ha sido creado. Ahora puede iniciar sesión.',
                });
                // The revalidation on the server action will refresh the page
            } else {
                toast({
                    title: 'Error',
                    description: result.message,
                    variant: 'destructive',
                });
            }
        } catch (error) {
             toast({
                title: 'Error de Sistema',
                description: 'No se pudo comunicar con el servidor.',
                variant: 'destructive',
            });
        } finally {
            setIsLoading(false);
        }
    };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-4 bg-gradient-to-br from-background to-secondary/30">
      <Card className="w-full max-w-md shadow-2xl">
        <CardHeader className="text-center">
            <div className="mx-auto mb-4">
               <UserPlus className="h-16 w-16 text-primary" />
            </div>
            <CardTitle className="text-3xl font-bold">Configuración Inicial</CardTitle>
            <CardDescription>
                Bienvenido. Por favor, cree el usuario administrador y configure el nombre de su empresa.
            </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
            <Form {...form}>
                <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="space-y-6">
                    <FormField
                        control={form.control}
                        name="companyName"
                        render={({ field }) => (
                            <FormItem>
                                <FormLabel>Nombre de la Empresa</FormLabel>
                                <FormControl>
                                    <Input placeholder="El nombre de su negocio" {...field} />
                                </FormControl>
                                <FormMessage />
                            </FormItem>
                        )}
                    />
                     <FormField
                        control={form.control}
                        name="username"
                        render={({ field }) => (
                            <FormItem>
                                <FormLabel>Nombre de Usuario Administrador</FormLabel>
                                <FormControl>
                                    <Input placeholder="admin" {...field} />
                                </FormControl>
                                <FormMessage />
                            </FormItem>
                        )}
                    />
                     <FormField
                        control={form.control}
                        name="password"
                        render={({ field }) => (
                            <FormItem>
                                <FormLabel>Contraseña</FormLabel>
                                <FormControl>
                                    <Input type="password" {...field} />
                                </FormControl>
                                <FormMessage />
                            </FormItem>
                        )}
                    />
                    <Button type="submit" className="w-full" disabled={isLoading}>
                        {isLoading && <LoadingSpinner className="mr-2" />}
                        Finalizar Configuración
                    </Button>
                </form>
            </Form>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
       <footer className="mt-8 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            <p>&copy; {new Date().getFullYear()} Clic Soporte & Clic Tienda S.R.L.</p>
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

--- File: src/components/auth/LoginForm.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useActionState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useFormStatus } from 'react-dom';
import { login } from '@/actions/authActions';
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { LogIn } from 'lucide-react';
import { useToast } from '@/hooks/use-toast';
import { LoadingSpinner } from '../common/LoadingSpinner';
import type { LicenseStatus } from '@/types/license';
import { Badge } from '../ui/badge';

function SubmitButton() {
    const { pending } = useFormStatus();
    return (
        <Button type="submit" className="w-full" disabled={pending}>
            {pending ? <LoadingSpinner className="mr-2" /> : <LogIn className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />}
            Iniciar Sesión
        </Button>
    );
}

export function LoginForm({ companyName, licenseStatus }: { companyName: string, licenseStatus: LicenseStatus }) {
    const [state, formAction] = useActionState(login, undefined);
    const { toast } = useToast();

    const licenseText = licenseStatus === 'VALID' ? 'Premium' : 'Gratuita';
    const licenseVariant = licenseStatus === 'VALID' ? 'default' : 'secondary';

    useEffect(() => {
        if (state?.success === false && state.message) {
            toast({
                title: 'Error de Inicio de Sesión',
                description: state.message,
                variant: 'destructive',
            });
        }
    }, [state, toast]);

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-4 bg-gradient-to-br from-background to-secondary/30">
      <Card className="w-full max-w-sm shadow-2xl">
        <CardHeader className="text-center">
            <div className="mx-auto mb-4">
                <LogIn className="h-16 w-16 text-primary" />
            </div>
            <CardTitle className="text-3xl font-bold">{companyName}</CardTitle>
            <CardDescription>
                Por favor, inicie sesión para continuar.
            </CardDescription>
            <div className="flex justify-center pt-2">
                <Badge variant={licenseVariant}>Licencia {licenseText}</Badge>
            </div>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
            <form action={formAction} className="space-y-4">
                <div className="space-y-2">
                    <Label htmlFor="username">Usuario</Label>
                    <Input id="username" name="username" placeholder="Su usuario" required />
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-2">
                    <Label htmlFor="password">Contraseña</Label>
                    <Input id="password" name="password" type="password" required />
                </div>
                <SubmitButton />
                 {state?.message && (
                    <p className="text-sm text-center text-destructive">{state.message}</p>
                 )}
            </form>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
      <footer className="mt-8 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            <p>&copy; {new Date().getFullYear()} Clic Soporte & Clic Tienda S.R.L.</p>
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

import { Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';

interface LoadingSpinnerProps {

  className?: string;

export function LoadingSpinner({ size = 24, className }: LoadingSpinnerProps) {

      className={cn('animate-spin text-primary', className)}

    />
  );

import type { LucideIcon } from 'lucide-react';

interface PageTitleProps {
  title: string;
  icon?: LucideIcon;
  className?: string;
  actions?: React.ReactNode;
}

export function PageTitle({ title, icon: Icon, className, actions }: PageTitleProps) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("flex items-center justify-between mb-8 pb-4 border-b", className)}>
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">

        </h1>
      </div>

--- File: src/components/display/DisplayScreenClient.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { getQueueStatus } from '@/actions/queueActions';
import { getExchangeRate } from '@/actions/settingsActions';
import type { QueueState } from '@/types/queue';
import type { AppSettings, ExchangeRateData } from '@/types/settings';
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Tv2, History, Users, Clock, DollarSign, User, HeartHandshake } from 'lucide-react';
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { ProductAdCarousel } from './ProductAd';
import { Skeleton } from '../ui/skeleton';

const AnimatedTicket = ({ ticketNumber, windowNumber, isManyWindows }: { ticketNumber: string | number, windowNumber?: string | number, isManyWindows?: boolean }) => (
  <motion.div
    key={`${ticketNumber}-${windowNumber || 'single'}`}
    initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
    animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
    exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
    transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
    className="text-center"
  >
    <p className={`leading-none font-extrabold text-primary ${isManyWindows ? 'text-6xl md:text-7xl' : 'text-8xl md:text-9xl'}`}>
      {ticketNumber}
    </p>
    {windowNumber && (
      <p className={`font-semibold text-secondary-foreground mt-1 ${isManyWindows ? 'text-2xl md:text-3xl' : 'text-4xl md:text-5xl'}`}>
        PUESTO {windowNumber}
      </p>
    )}
  </motion.div>
);

const ClockDisplay = () => {
    const [time, setTime] = useState(new Date());

    useEffect(() => {
        const timerId = setInterval(() => setTime(new Date()), 1000);
        return () => clearInterval(timerId);
    }, []);
    
    return (
       <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <Clock className="h-10 w-10" />
        <span className="font-mono text-5xl font-semibold tabular-nums">
            {time.toLocaleTimeString('es-CR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}
        </span>
       </div>
    );
};


export function DisplayScreenClient({ initialQueueState, settings, initialExchangeRate }: { initialQueueState: QueueState, settings: AppSettings, initialExchangeRate: ExchangeRateData | null }) {
  const [queueState, setQueueState] = useState<QueueState>(initialQueueState);
  const [exchangeRate, setExchangeRate] = useState<ExchangeRateData | null>(initialExchangeRate);
  const [lastUpdateTime, setLastUpdateTime] = useState<Date | null>(null);
  const [isClient, setIsClient] = useState(false);

  const companyName = settings.companyName || "Clic Tienda Turnos";

  useEffect(() => {
    setIsClient(true);
  }, []);

  const fetchAndUpdateState = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const newState = await getQueueStatus();
      setQueueState(newState);
      setLastUpdateTime(new Date());

    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching queue status for display:", error);
    }
  }, []);

  const fetchExchangeRate = useCallback(async () => {
    if (settings.showExchangeRate) {
      try {
        const newRate = await getExchangeRate();
        setExchangeRate(newRate);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Error fetching exchange rate for display:", error);
        setExchangeRate(null);
      }
    }
  }, [settings.showExchangeRate]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchAndUpdateState(); 
    const stateIntervalId = setInterval(fetchAndUpdateState, 5000); 
    
    fetchExchangeRate();
    const exchangeRateIntervalId = setInterval(fetchExchangeRate, 3600000); // Update exchange rate every hour
    
    return () => {
      clearInterval(stateIntervalId);
      clearInterval(exchangeRateIntervalId);
    }
  }, [fetchAndUpdateState, fetchExchangeRate]);

  const { nowServing, activeWindows, operationMode, recentlyCalled, tickets, availableWindows } = queueState;
  const waitingGeneral = tickets.filter(t => t.status === 'waiting' && t.type === 'general').length;
  const waitingPreferential = tickets.filter(t => t.status === 'waiting' && t.type === 'preferential').length;

  const isMultiWindowMany = operationMode === 'multi' && availableWindows.length >= 4;
  
  const gridColsClasses: { [key: number]: string } = {
    1: 'sm:grid-cols-1',
    2: 'sm:grid-cols-2',
    3: 'sm:grid-cols-3',
  };
  const multiWindowGridCols = availableWindows.length <= 3 
    ? gridColsClasses[availableWindows.length] || 'sm:grid-cols-3'
    : 'sm:grid-cols-3';


  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-background to-secondary/30 text-foreground">
      <div className="flex-grow p-4 md:p-8 flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
        <header className="w-full max-w-7xl mx-auto mb-6 md:mb-8 flex justify-between items-center">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <Tv2 className="h-12 w-12 text-primary" />
            <div>
                <h1 className="text-2xl md:text-3xl font-bold tracking-tight text-primary">
                {companyName}
                </h1>
                <p className="text-sm md:text-base text-muted-foreground">Estado de la Cola en Tiempo Real</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="text-right text-muted-foreground">
             {isClient && <ClockDisplay />}
             {settings.showExchangeRate && (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-2">
                    <DollarSign className="h-10 w-10" />
                    {isClient && exchangeRate ? (
                         <span className="font-mono text-3xl font-medium">
                            C: {exchangeRate.compra.toFixed(2)} | V: {exchangeRate.venta.toFixed(2)}
                         </span>
                    ) : isClient ? null : (
                        <Skeleton className="h-8 w-60" />
                    )}
                </div>
             )}
          </div>
        </header>

        <main className="w-full max-w-7xl mx-auto grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6 md:gap-8 flex-grow">
          <Card className="lg:col-span-2 shadow-xl rounded-2xl p-6 md:p-8 bg-card">
            <CardHeader className="pb-4 text-center">
              <CardTitle className="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-semibold text-card-foreground">
                TURNO ACTUAL / NOW SERVING
              </CardTitle>
            </CardHeader>
            <CardContent className={`flex items-center justify-center ${isMultiWindowMany ? 'h-auto min-h-[280px] md:min-h-[320px]' : 'h-[250px] md:h-[300px]'}`}>
              <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
                {operationMode === 'single' && nowServing && (
                  <AnimatedTicket ticketNumber={nowServing.displayNumber} />
                )}
                {operationMode === 'single' && !nowServing && (
                   <motion.p  initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }} className="text-3xl text-muted-foreground">Esperando llamada...</motion.p>
                )}
                {operationMode === 'multi' && Object.values(activeWindows).every(t => t === null) && availableWindows.length > 0 && (
                   <motion.p initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }} className="text-3xl text-muted-foreground">Puestos libres o esperando...</motion.p>
                )}
                 {operationMode === 'multi' && availableWindows.length === 0 && (
                   <motion.p initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }} className="text-xl text-muted-foreground">No hay puestos configurados. Por favor, configure los puestos en la consola de asistente.</motion.p>
                )}
              </AnimatePresence>
              {operationMode === 'multi' && availableWindows.length > 0 && (
                <div className={`grid grid-cols-1 ${multiWindowGridCols} gap-2 md:gap-4 w-full`}>
                  {availableWindows.map(winNum => {
                     const ticket = activeWindows[winNum];
                     return (
                      <div key={winNum} className={`p-3 md:p-4 rounded-lg text-center border-2 ${ticket ? 'border-primary bg-primary/10' : 'border-dashed border-muted-foreground/30'}`}>
                        <p className={`font-medium text-muted-foreground ${isMultiWindowMany ? 'text-lg md:text-xl' : 'text-xl'}`}>PUESTO {winNum}</p>
                         <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
                          {ticket ? (
                             <AnimatedTicket ticketNumber={ticket.displayNumber} isManyWindows={isMultiWindowMany} />
                          ) : (
                            <motion.p 
                              initial={{ opacity: 0 }} 
                              animate={{ opacity: 1 }} 
                              exit={{ opacity: 0 }} 
                              className={`font-bold text-muted-foreground/50 ${isMultiWindowMany ? 'text-4xl py-6 md:py-8' : 'text-5xl py-8'}`}
                            >
                              -
                            </motion.p>
                          )}
                        </AnimatePresence>
                      </div>
                     );
                  })}
                </div>
              )}
            </CardContent>
          </Card>

          <div className="space-y-6 md:space-y-8">
            <Card className="shadow-xl rounded-2xl bg-card">
              <CardHeader className="pb-2">
                 <CardTitle className="text-lg font-medium text-card-foreground">En Espera</CardTitle>
              </CardHeader>
              <CardContent className='flex justify-around items-center'>
                  <div className='text-center'>
                     <Users className="h-5 w-5 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-1" />
                     <div className="text-4xl font-bold text-primary">{waitingGeneral}</div>
                     <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Generales</p>
                  </div>
                   <div className='text-center'>
                     <HeartHandshake className="h-5 w-5 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-1" />
                     <div className="text-4xl font-bold text-blue-600">{waitingPreferential}</div>
                     <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Preferenciales</p>
                  </div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>

            <Card className="shadow-xl rounded-2xl bg-card">
              <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
                <CardTitle className="text-lg font-medium text-card-foreground">Últimas Llamadas</CardTitle>
                <History className="h-5 w-5 text-muted-foreground" />
              </CardHeader>
              <CardContent>
                {recentlyCalled.length > 0 ? (
                  <ul className="space-y-2">
                    <AnimatePresence>
                      {recentlyCalled.slice(0, 3).map((ticket, index) => (
                        <motion.li
                          key={ticket.id}
                          initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
                          animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                          transition={{ delay: index * 0.1, duration: 0.3 }}
                          className="text-lg text-secondary-foreground flex justify-between items-baseline"
                        >
                          <div className="flex items-baseline gap-3">
                              <span>Ticket <span className="font-bold">{ticket.displayNumber}</span></span>
                              {ticket.window && <span className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground">(P.{ticket.window})</span>}
                          </div>
                          {ticket.callTimestamp && isClient && (
                              <span className="text-sm font-mono text-muted-foreground">
                                  {new Date(ticket.callTimestamp).toLocaleTimeString('es-CR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', second: '2-digit' })}
                              </span>
                          )}
                        </motion.li>
                      ))}
                    </AnimatePresence>
                  </ul>
                ) : (
                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">No hay llamadas recientes.</p>
                )}
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
          </div>
        </main>
      </div>
      <div className="w-full max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4">
        <ProductAdCarousel 
          isAdFeatureEnabled={settings.isAdFeatureEnabled ?? false}
          ads={settings.adCarouselItems ?? []}
        />
      </div>
      <footer className="w-full text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground py-2">
        <div className="flex justify-center items-center gap-x-4 flex-wrap">
            {lastUpdateTime && isClient && (
                <span>Última actualización: {lastUpdateTime.toLocaleTimeString('es-CR')} (Cola v{queueState._version})</span>
            )}
            <span>&copy; {new Date().getFullYear()} {companyName}</span>
            <span className='font-mono'>{settings.appVersion}</span>
            <a href="https://clictienda.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" className="hover:underline">www.clictienda.com</a>
            <a href="mailto:ventas@clicsoporte.com" className="hover:underline">ventas@clicsoporte.com</a>
            <span>Telf: +506 4000 0630</span>
        </div>
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

--- File: src/components/display/ProductAd.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import Image from 'next/image';
import { Card, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Skeleton } from '@/components/ui/skeleton';
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { ShoppingCart, ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-react';
import type { AdCarouselItem } from '@/types/settings';
import { Button } from '../ui/button';


interface ProductAdCarouselProps {
  isAdFeatureEnabled: boolean;
  ads: AdCarouselItem[];
}

const AD_REFRESH_INTERVAL = 10000; // 10 segundos

export function ProductAdCarousel({ isAdFeatureEnabled, ads }: ProductAdCarouselProps) {
  const [currentIndex, setCurrentIndex] = useState(0);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isAdFeatureEnabled || !ads || ads.length === 0) return;

    const intervalId = setInterval(() => {
      setCurrentIndex((prevIndex) => (prevIndex + 1) % ads.length);
    }, AD_REFRESH_INTERVAL);

    return () => clearInterval(intervalId);
  }, [ads, isAdFeatureEnabled]);

  const goToPrevious = () => {
    setCurrentIndex((prevIndex) => (prevIndex - 1 + ads.length) % ads.length);
  };

  const goToNext = () => {
     setCurrentIndex((prevIndex) => (prevIndex + 1) % ads.length);
  };

  if (!isAdFeatureEnabled || !ads || ads.length === 0) {
    return (
        <div className="w-full max-w-5xl mx-auto p-4">
            <Card className="bg-card/70 backdrop-blur-sm border-border/50">
                <CardContent className="p-4 flex items-center justify-center gap-4 h-[120px]">
                    <ShoppingCart className="h-6 w-6 text-muted-foreground" />
                    <p className="text-muted-foreground">La publicidad está desactivada o no hay anuncios configurados.</p>
                </CardContent>
            </Card>
        </div>
    );
  }
  
  const ad = ads[currentIndex];

  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-7xl mx-auto p-4 relative">
       <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
          <motion.div
            key={currentIndex}
            initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 50 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, x: -50 }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
            className="w-full"
          >
            <Card className="bg-card/70 backdrop-blur-sm border-border/50 shadow-lg overflow-hidden">
                <CardContent className="p-2 sm:p-4 flex flex-col sm:flex-row items-center gap-4">
                   <div className="relative h-24 w-24 flex-shrink-0">
                     <Image
                       src={ad.imageUrl}
                       alt={ad.description}
                       fill
                       className="object-cover rounded-md"
                       sizes="(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 96px"
                       data-ai-hint="advertisement image"
                       unoptimized
                     />
                   </div>
                   <div className="text-center sm:text-left flex-1">
                       <p className="text-sm text-card-foreground line-clamp-2">{ad.description}</p>
                   </div>
                   <div className="flex-shrink-0 text-center sm:text-right">
                       <p className="text-2xl font-extrabold text-accent-foreground">{ad.price}</p>
                   </div>
                </CardContent>
            </Card>
          </motion.div>
      </AnimatePresence>
      {ads.length > 1 && (
        <>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="absolute left-0 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2" onClick={goToPrevious}>
                <ChevronLeft className="h-6 w-6" />
            </Button>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="absolute right-0 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2" onClick={goToNext}>
                <ChevronRight className="h-6 w-6" />
            </Button>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

--- File: src/components/kiosk/KioskClient.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { issueTicket, getQueueStatus } from '@/actions/queueActions';
import type { QueueState, Ticket, TicketType } from '@/types/queue';
import type { AppSettings } from '@/types/settings';
import { TicketModal } from './TicketModal';
import { LoadingSpinner } from '@/components/common/LoadingSpinner';
import { TicketIcon, Ban, User, HeartHandshake } from 'lucide-react';
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { Separator } from '../ui/separator';

export function KioskClient({ initialQueueState, settings }: { initialQueueState: QueueState, settings: AppSettings }) {
  const [issuedTicket, setIssuedTicket] = useState<Ticket | null>(null);
  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [currentQueueState, setCurrentQueueState] = useState<QueueState>(initialQueueState);
  const { toast } = useToast();

  const companyName = settings.companyName || "Clic Tienda Turnos";

  const fetchAndUpdateState = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const newState = await getQueueStatus();
      setCurrentQueueState(newState);
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn("Kiosk: Error polling for queue state.", error);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchAndUpdateState(); // Initial fetch on mount
    const intervalId = setInterval(fetchAndUpdateState, 10000); // Poll every 10 seconds
    return () => clearInterval(intervalId);
  }, [fetchAndUpdateState]);

  const handleIssueTicket = async (type: TicketType) => {
    if (currentQueueState.manualDispenserMode) {
      toast({
        title: "Modo Manual Activo",
        description: "El sistema está configurado para dispensar tickets físicos manualmente.",
        variant: "default",
      });
      return;
    }
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const result = await issueTicket(type);
      if (result.success && result.ticket && result.updatedState) {
        setIssuedTicket(result.ticket);
        setIsModalOpen(true);
        setCurrentQueueState(result.updatedState);
        toast({
          title: "Ticket Emitido",
          description: `Su número de ticket es ${result.ticket.displayNumber}.`,
        });
      } else {
        toast({
          title: "Error",
          description: result.message || "No se pudo emitir el ticket.",
          variant: "destructive",
        });
        if (result.updatedState) {
          setCurrentQueueState(result.updatedState);
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast({
        title: "Error de Sistema",
        description: "Ocurrió un error al contactar el servidor.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const manualModeActive = currentQueueState.manualDispenserMode;

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-4 sm:p-8 bg-gradient-to-br from-background to-secondary/30">
      <Card className="w-full max-w-xl shadow-2xl rounded-xl bg-card">
        <CardHeader className="text-center">
          <div className="mx-auto mb-4">
            {manualModeActive ? <Ban className="h-20 w-20 text-muted-foreground" /> : <TicketIcon className="h-20 w-20 text-primary" />}
          </div>
          <CardTitle className="text-4xl font-bold text-primary">{companyName}</CardTitle>
          <CardDescription className="text-lg text-muted-foreground mt-2">
            {manualModeActive
              ? "Dispensador de tickets manual activo. Por favor, tome un ticket físico."
              : "Bienvenido. Toque el botón para obtener su número de turno."}
          </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent className="p-8">
          {manualModeActive ? (
            <Button
              className="w-full h-24 text-3xl font-semibold rounded-lg"
              disabled={true}
              aria-label="Modo Manual"
            >
              <Ban className="mr-4 h-10 w-10" />
              Modo Manual
            </Button>
          ) : (
            <div className="space-y-6">
              <Button
                onClick={() => handleIssueTicket('general')}
                className="w-full h-24 text-3xl font-semibold rounded-lg bg-accent text-accent-foreground hover:bg-accent/90 shadow-lg transform transition-transform hover:scale-105"
                disabled={isLoading}
                aria-label="Obtener Ticket General"
              >
                {isLoading ? <LoadingSpinner size={40} /> : (
                  <>
                    <User className="mr-4 h-10 w-10" />
                    Tiquete General
                  </>
                )}
              </Button>
              <Separator />
              <Button
                onClick={() => handleIssueTicket('preferential')}
                className="w-full h-24 text-3xl font-semibold rounded-lg bg-blue-500 text-white hover:bg-blue-600 shadow-lg transform transition-transform hover:scale-105"
                disabled={isLoading}
                aria-label="Obtener Ticket Preferencial"
              >
                {isLoading ? <LoadingSpinner size={40} /> : (
                   <>
                    <HeartHandshake className="mr-4 h-10 w-10" />
                    Tiquete Preferencial
                  </>
                )}
              </Button>
            </div>
          )}
          <p className="text-xs text-center mt-6 text-muted-foreground">
            Cola v{currentQueueState._version}
          </p>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {issuedTicket && !manualModeActive && (
        <TicketModal
          ticket={issuedTicket}
          isOpen={isModalOpen}
          onClose={() => setIsModalOpen(false)}
          companyName={companyName}
        />
      )}

      <footer className="mt-12 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
        <p>&copy; {new Date().getFullYear()} Clic Soporte & Clic Tienda S.R.L. Todos los derechos reservados.</p>
        <p className='font-mono text-xs mt-1'>{settings.appVersion}</p>
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

--- File: src/components/kiosk/TicketModal.tsx ---

"use client";

import type { Ticket } from '@/types/queue';
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle, DialogDescription } from '@/components/ui/dialog';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Printer, TicketIcon as TicketDisplayIcon } from 'lucide-react'; 

interface TicketModalProps {
  ticket: Ticket | null;
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  companyName?: string;
}

export function TicketModal({ ticket, isOpen, onClose, companyName = "Clic Tienda Turnos" }: TicketModalProps) {
  if (!ticket) return null;

  const handlePrint = () => {
    const printContent = `
      <html>
        <head>
          <title>Ticket ${ticket.displayNumber}</title>
          <style>
            body { font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif; text-align: center; margin: 0; padding: 20px; width: 300px; box-sizing: border-box; }
            .header { font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 5px; }
            .ticket-number-label { font-size: 18px; margin: 5px 0; }
            .ticket-number { font-size: 48px; font-weight: bold; margin: 5px 0 10px 0; }
            .timestamp { font-size: 14px; margin-bottom: 10px; }
            .instructions { font-size: 14px; margin-bottom: 15px; }
            .branding { font-size: 10px; margin-top: 15px; line-height: 1.2; }
            .branding a { color: #000; text-decoration: none; }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <div class="header">${companyName}</div>
          <p class="ticket-number-label">Su Turno / Your Turn</p>
          <h1 class="ticket-number">${ticket.displayNumber}</h1>
          <p class="timestamp">Emitido: ${new Date(ticket.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}</p>
          <p class="instructions">Por favor, espere su llamada.</p>
          <div class="branding">
            www.clictienda.com<br/>
            ventas@clicsoporte.com<br/>
            Telf: +506 4000 0630
          </div>
        </body>
      </html>
    `;
    const printWindow = window.open('', '_blank');
    if (printWindow) {
      printWindow.document.write(printContent);
      printWindow.document.close();
      printWindow.focus(); 
      setTimeout(() => {
        printWindow.print();
      }, 250); 
    } else {
      alert("Por favor, habilite las ventanas emergentes para imprimir su ticket.");
    }
    onClose(); 
  };


  return (
    <Dialog open={isOpen} onOpenChange={onClose}>
      <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md bg-card text-card-foreground p-6 rounded-lg shadow-xl">
        <DialogHeader className="mb-4">
          <DialogTitle className="text-3xl font-bold text-center text-primary flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
            <TicketDisplayIcon className="h-8 w-8" />
            Su Ticket / Your Ticket
          </DialogTitle>
          <DialogDescription className="text-center text-muted-foreground mt-2">
            Guarde este número. Será llamado pronto.
            <br />
            Save this number. You will be called soon.
          </DialogDescription>
        </DialogHeader>
        
        <div className="text-center my-8">
          <p className="text-lg text-foreground">Número de Ticket / Ticket Number:</p>
          <p className="text-8xl font-extrabold text-primary my-4 animate-pulse">
            {ticket.displayNumber}
          </p>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            Emitido / Issued: {new Date(ticket.timestamp).toLocaleString()}
          </p>
        </div>

        <div className="mt-6 flex flex-col gap-3">
           <Button onClick={handlePrint} variant="default" className="w-full bg-accent text-accent-foreground hover:bg-accent/90 py-3 text-lg">
            <Printer className="mr-2 h-5 w-5" />
            Imprimir Ticket / Print Ticket
          </Button>
          <Button onClick={onClose} variant="outline" className="w-full py-3 text-lg">
            Cerrar / Close
          </Button>
        </div>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}

"use client";

import { useState, useRef, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { useForm, FormProvider, useFormContext } from 'react-hook-form';
import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
import * as z from 'zod';
import { Button, buttonVariants } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Card, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Form, FormControl, FormField, FormItem, FormLabel, FormMessage, FormDescription as FormDesc } from '@/components/ui/form';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Textarea } from '@/components/ui/textarea';
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { PageTitle } from '@/components/common/PageTitle';
import { Home, Save, Loader2, Landmark, RefreshCw, Building, ListCollapse, ListX, Shield, Download, UploadCloud, KeyRound, UserCog, VenetianMask, Database, Eraser, Factory, LifeBuoy, GitBranchPlus, CloudDownload, TerminalSquare, Info, Server, Power } from 'lucide-react';
import type { AppSettings } from '@/types/settings';
import { updateSettings, checkForUpdates } from '@/actions/settingsActions';
import { refreshAllModules } from '@/actions/queueActions';
import { getLogs, clearLogs } from '@/actions/logActions';
import { backupDatabase, restoreDatabase, purgeHistoricalData, restoreFactorySettings, getSystemStats, type SystemStats } from '@/actions/systemActions';
import { AlertDialog, AlertDialogAction, AlertDialogCancel, AlertDialogContent, AlertDialogDescription, AlertDialogFooter, AlertDialogHeader, AlertDialogTitle, AlertDialogTrigger } from "@/components/ui/alert-dialog";
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogDescription, DialogHeader, DialogTitle, DialogFooter, DialogClose } from "@/components/ui/dialog";

const settingsSchema = z.object({
  companyName: z.string().min(1, "El nombre de la empresa es requerido."),
  companyId: z.string().optional(),
  contactPhone: z.string().optional(),
  contactEmail: z.string().email({ message: "Por favor, ingrese un email válido." }).optional().or(z.literal('')),
  country: z.string().optional(),
  address: z.string().optional(),
  branchName: z.string().optional(),
  licenseKey: z.string().optional(),
  licenseServerDomain: z.string().url({ message: "Debe ser una URL de dominio válida." }).optional().or(z.literal('')),
  supportTicketEmbedCode: z.string().optional(),
  gitRepositoryUrl: z.string().url({ message: "Debe ser una URL de repositorio Git válida." }).optional().or(z.literal('')),
  exchangeRateApiUrl: z.string().url({ message: "Por favor, ingrese una URL de API válida." }).optional().or(z.literal('')),
});

type SettingsFormValues = z.infer<typeof settingsSchema>;

const SUPER_ADMIN_UNLOCK_PASSWORD = "Clic2017*";
const SUPER_ADMIN_UNLOCK_CLICKS = 10;

function SystemStatus() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<SystemStats | null>(null);
  const [isStatsLoading, setIsStatsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const {toast} = useToast();

  const fetchStats = useCallback(async () => {
    setIsStatsLoading(true);
    try {
      const systemStats = await getSystemStats();
      setStats(systemStats);
    } catch (error) {
       toast({ title: "Error al Cargar Estadísticas", description: "No se pudo obtener el estado del sistema.", variant: "destructive" });
       setStats(null);
    } finally {
      setIsStatsLoading(false);
    }
  }, [toast]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchStats();
  }, [fetchStats]);

  const handleRefreshCache = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
     try {
      await refreshAllModules();
      toast({ title: "Actualización Solicitada", description: "Se ha solicitado una actualización de caché para todos los módulos." });
    } catch (error) {
      toast({ title: "Error de Sistema", variant: "destructive" });
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <AccordionItem value="system-status">
      <AccordionTrigger className="text-lg font-semibold px-6">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2"><Server /> Estado del Sistema</div>
      </AccordionTrigger>
      <AccordionContent className="px-6 pb-6 space-y-4">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
             <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground -mt-2 mb-2">
                Métricas de salud y rendimiento del servidor.
             </p>
             <Button onClick={fetchStats} variant="ghost" size="icon" disabled={isStatsLoading}>
                <RefreshCw className={`h-4 w-4 ${isStatsLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
             </Button>
        </div>
        
        {isStatsLoading ? (
            <div className="flex justify-center items-center h-24">
                <Loader2 className="animate-spin h-8 w-8 text-primary" />
            </div>
        ) : stats ? (
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-sm">
                <div className="p-3 bg-muted/30 rounded-lg"><strong>Uso de CPU:</strong> {stats.cpuUsage}</div>
                <div className="p-3 bg-muted/30 rounded-lg"><strong>Uptime:</strong> {stats.uptime}</div>
                <div className="p-3 bg-muted/30 rounded-lg col-span-2"><strong>Uso de Memoria:</strong> {stats.memoryUsage}</div>
                <div className="p-3 bg-muted/30 rounded-lg col-span-2"><strong>Uso de Disco:</strong> {stats.diskUsage}</div>
            </div>
        ) : (
            <p className="text-destructive text-center">No se pudieron cargar las estadísticas del sistema.</p>
        )}

        <Separator/>
        <Button onClick={handleRefreshCache} disabled={isLoading} variant="outline" type="button" className="w-full">
            {isLoading ? <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin"/> : <Power className="mr-2 h-4 w-4"/>}
            Forzar Actualización de Caché Global
        </Button>
      </AccordionContent>
    </AccordionItem>
  )
}

export function SettingsClient({ initialSettings, currentUser }: { initialSettings: AppSettings, currentUser: SessionUser }) {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const [isSaving, setIsSaving] = useState(false);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<LogEntry[]>([]);
  const [isLogLoading, setIsLogLoading] = useState(false);
  const restoreFileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const [isSuperAdminDialogOpen, setIsSuperAdminDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const [passwordInput, setPasswordInput] = useState("");
  const [passwordUnlocked, setPasswordUnlocked] = useState(false);
  const [adminClickCount, setAdminClickCount] = useState(0);
  const [isClient, setIsClient] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    setIsClient(true);
  }, []);

  const isSuperAdmin = currentUser?.role === 'superadmin';

  const formMethods = useForm<SettingsFormValues>({
    resolver: zodResolver(settingsSchema),
    defaultValues: {
      companyName: initialSettings.companyName ?? "CLIC SOPORTE & CLIC TIENDA S.R.L",
      companyId: initialSettings.companyId ?? "",
      contactPhone: initialSettings.contactPhone ?? "",
      contactEmail: initialSettings.contactEmail ?? "",
      country: initialSettings.country ?? "",
      address: initialSettings.address ?? "",
      branchName: initialSettings.branchName ?? "",
      licenseKey: initialSettings.licenseKey ?? '',
      licenseServerDomain: initialSettings.licenseServerDomain ?? 'https://licencias.clicsoporte.com',
      supportTicketEmbedCode: initialSettings.supportTicketEmbedCode ?? '',
      gitRepositoryUrl: initialSettings.gitRepositoryUrl ?? '',
      exchangeRateApiUrl: initialSettings.exchangeRateApiUrl ?? "https://api.hacienda.go.cr/indicadores/tc",
    },
  });

  const onSubmit = async (values: SettingsFormValues) => {
    setIsSaving(true);
    try {
        const result = await updateSettings(values);

      if (result.success) {
        toast({
          title: "Configuración Guardada",
          description: "La configuración ha sido actualizada correctamente.",
        });
        if (result.updatedSettings) {
            formMethods.reset(result.updatedSettings);
        }
      } else {
        toast({
          title: "Error al Guardar",
          description: result.message || "No se pudo guardar la configuración.",
          variant: "destructive",
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast({
        title: "Error de Sistema",
        description: "Ocurrió un error de comunicación.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    } finally {
      setIsSaving(false);
    }
  };
  
  const handleFetchLogs = async () => {
    setIsLogLoading(true);
    try {
        const fetchedLogs = await getLogs();
        setLogs(fetchedLogs);
        toast({ title: "Logs Cargados", description: `Se encontraron ${fetchedLogs.length} eventos.` });
    } catch(e) {
        toast({ title: "Error al Cargar Logs", variant: "destructive" });
    } finally {
        setIsLogLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const handleClearLogs = async () => {
    setIsLogLoading(true);
    try {
        await clearLogs();
        setLogs([]);
        toast({ title: "Logs Limpiados" });
    } catch (e) {
        toast({ title: "Error al Limpiar Logs", variant: "destructive" });
    } finally {
        setIsLogLoading(false);
    }
  };
  
  const handleDownloadLogs = () => {
    const logContent = logs
      .map(log => `[${log.type.toUpperCase()}] ${new Date(log.timestamp).toLocaleString()} [${log.context}]\n${log.message}${log.details ? `\nDETAILS: ${JSON.stringify(log.details)}` : ''}`)
      .join('\n\n');
    
    const blob = new Blob([logContent], { type: 'text/plain;charset=utf-8' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = url;
    link.download = `clic-soporte-logs-${new Date().toISOString()}.txt`;
    document.body.appendChild(link);
    link.click();
    document.body.removeChild(link);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  };

  const handleSuperAdminLinkClick = () => {
    if (isSuperAdmin || passwordUnlocked) {
      setIsSuperAdminDialogOpen(true);
      return;
    }
    
    const newClickCount = adminClickCount + 1;
    setAdminClickCount(newClickCount);

    if (newClickCount >= SUPER_ADMIN_UNLOCK_CLICKS) {
      const password = prompt("Ingrese la contraseña de Super Administrador:");
      if (password === SUPER_ADMIN_UNLOCK_PASSWORD) {
        setPasswordUnlocked(true);
        setIsSuperAdminDialogOpen(true);
        toast({ title: "Acceso Concedido", description: "Sección de Clic Soporte Admin desbloqueada." });
      } else if (password !== null) {
        toast({ title: "Acceso Denegado", variant: "destructive" });
      }
      setAdminClickCount(0);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    formMethods.reset(initialSettings);
  }, [initialSettings, formMethods]);
  
  
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-background to-secondary/30">
      <div className="container mx-auto p-4 md:p-8 flex-grow">
        <PageTitle title="Configuración del Sistema" icon={Landmark} actions={
          <Link href="/" passHref legacyBehavior>
            <Button variant="outline"><Home className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Menú Principal</Button>
          </Link>
        } />

        {!isClient ? (
            <SettingsSkeleton />
        ) : (
            <FormProvider {...formMethods}>
            <form onSubmit={formMethods.handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="space-y-8">
                <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-8 items-start">
                
                <div className="lg:col-span-1 space-y-8">
                    <Card className="shadow-lg rounded-xl bg-card">
                    <CardContent className="p-0">
                        <Accordion type="single" collapsible className="w-full" defaultValue='item-1'>
                            <AccordionItem value="item-1">
                                <AccordionTrigger className="text-lg font-semibold px-6"><div className="flex items-center gap-2"><Building /> General</div></AccordionTrigger>
                                <AccordionContent className="px-6 pb-6 space-y-4">
                                <FormField
                                    control={formMethods.control}
                                    name="companyName"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Nombre de la Empresa</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="El nombre de tu empresa" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                    />
                                    <FormField
                                    control={formMethods.control}
                                    name="companyId"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>ID / Cédula Jurídica</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="Ej: 3-101-..." {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                    />
                                    <FormField
                                    control={formMethods.control}
                                    name="contactPhone"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Teléfono de Contacto</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="+506 8888 8888" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                    />
                                    <FormField
                                    control={formMethods.control}
                                    name="contactEmail"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Email de Contacto</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input type="email" placeholder="contacto@empresa.com" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                    />
                                    <FormField
                                    control={formMethods.control}
                                    name="country"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>País</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="Costa Rica" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                    />
                                    <FormField
                                    control={formMethods.control}
                                    name="address"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Dirección</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Textarea placeholder="Dirección física de la empresa" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                    />
                                    <FormField
                                    control={formMethods.control}
                                    name="branchName"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Nombre de la Sucursal (Opcional)</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="Ej: San José Centro" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                    />
                                </AccordionContent>
                            </AccordionItem>
                        </Accordion>
                    </CardContent>
                    </Card>
                </div>

                <div className="lg:col-span-2 space-y-8">
                    <Card className="shadow-lg rounded-xl bg-card">
                    <CardContent className="p-0">
                        <Accordion type="single" collapsible className="w-full">
                        <AccordionItem value="item-1">
                            <AccordionTrigger className="text-lg font-semibold px-6"><div className="flex items-center gap-2"><ListCollapse /> Visor de Eventos del Sistema</div></AccordionTrigger>
                            <AccordionContent className="space-y-4 px-6 pb-6">
                                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground -mt-2 mb-2">
                                Aquí se registran eventos importantes y errores del sistema.
                                </p>
                                <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
                                    <Button onClick={handleFetchLogs} disabled={isLogLoading} variant="outline" type="button">
                                        {isLogLoading ? <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin"/> : <RefreshCw className="mr-2 h-4 w-4"/>}
                                        Cargar Eventos
                                    </Button>
                                    <Button onClick={handleDownloadLogs} disabled={isLogLoading || logs.length === 0} variant="outline" type="button">
                                        <Download className="mr-2 h-4 w-4"/>
                                        Descargar Logs
                                    </Button>
                                    <AlertDialog>
                                        <AlertDialogTrigger asChild>
                                            <Button disabled={isLogLoading || logs.length === 0} variant="destructive" type="button"><ListX className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />Limpiar Eventos</Button>
                                        </AlertDialogTrigger>
                                        <AlertDialogContent>
                                            <AlertDialogHeader><AlertDialogTitle>¿Está seguro?</AlertDialogTitle><AlertDialogDescription>Esta acción borrará permanentemente todos los registros de eventos. No se puede deshacer.</AlertDialogDescription></AlertDialogHeader>
                                            <AlertDialogFooter>
                                                <AlertDialogCancel>Cancelar</AlertDialogCancel>
                                                <AlertDialogAction onClick={handleClearLogs} className={cn(buttonVariants({variant: "destructive"}))}>Confirmar Borrado</AlertDialogAction>
                                            </AlertDialogFooter>
                                        </AlertDialogContent>
                                    </AlertDialog>
                                </div>
                                <ScrollArea className="h-72 w-full rounded-md border p-2 bg-muted/20">
                                {logs.length > 0 ? (
