                                    <div className="space-y-2 p-2">
                                    {logs.map((log) => (
                                        <div key={log.id} className="text-xs font-mono p-2 rounded-md bg-background shadow-sm">
                                        <div className={cn(
                                            "font-bold flex items-center gap-2",
                                            log.type === 'error' && 'text-red-500',
                                            log.type === 'warn' && 'text-yellow-500',
                                            log.type === 'info' && 'text-blue-500'
                                        )}>
                                            <span>[{log.type.toUpperCase()}]</span>
                                            <span>{new Date(log.timestamp).toLocaleString()}</span>
                                            <span>[{log.context}]</span>
                                        </div>
                                        <p className="pl-2 whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">{log.message}</p>
                                        {log.details && <p className="pl-2 text-xs opacity-70 break-all">Detalles: {JSON.stringify(log.details)}</p>}
                                        </div>
                                    ))}
                                    </div>
                                ) : (
                                    <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full">
                                        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">No hay eventos para mostrar.</p>
                                    </div>
                                )}
                                </ScrollArea>
                            </AccordionContent>
                            </AccordionItem>
                            {isClient && <SystemStatus />}
                        </Accordion>
                    </CardContent>
                    </Card>
                </div>
                </div>
                
                <div className="flex justify-end mt-8">
                <Button type="submit" disabled={isSaving || isLoading} className="w-full lg:w-auto">
                    {isSaving ? <><Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />Guardando...</> : <><Save className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />Guardar Configuración General</>}
                </Button>
                </div>
            </form>
            <Dialog open={isSuperAdminDialogOpen} onOpenChange={setIsSuperAdminDialogOpen}>
              <DialogContent className="max-w-4xl h-[90vh] flex flex-col">
                  <DialogHeader>
                      <DialogTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-amber-600"><VenetianMask/> Clic Soporte Admin</DialogTitle>
                      <DialogDescription>
                          Esta sección es para la administración remota de Clic Soporte. Los cambios aquí deben realizarse con precaución.
                      </DialogDescription>
                  </DialogHeader>
                  <FormProvider {...formMethods}>
                    <div className="flex-grow overflow-y-auto pr-6 -mr-6 space-y-6">
                      <SuperAdminContent
                          initialSettings={initialSettings}
                          isLoading={isLoading}
                          setIsLoading={setIsLoading}
                          restoreFileInputRef={restoreFileInputRef}
                      />
                    </div>
                    <DialogFooter className='!justify-between'>
                        <Button type="submit" form="settings-form" disabled={isSaving || isLoading} onClick={() => formMethods.handleSubmit(onSubmit)()}>
                            {isSaving ? <><Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />Guardando...</> : <><Save className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />Guardar Cambios</>}
                        </Button>
                        <DialogClose asChild>
                            <Button variant="outline" type="button">Cerrar</Button>
                        </DialogClose>
                    </DialogFooter>
                  </FormProvider>
              </DialogContent>
            </Dialog>
            </FormProvider>
        )}
      </div>
       <footer className="w-full text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground py-8">
        <div className="flex justify-center items-center gap-x-4 flex-wrap">
            <p>&copy; {new Date().getFullYear()} CLIC SOPORTE & CLIC TIENDA S.R.L.</p>
            <p className='font-mono text-xs'>{initialSettings.appVersion}</p>
            <span className="text-muted-foreground/50">|</span>
            <Button variant="link" className="p-0 h-auto text-muted-foreground" onClick={handleSuperAdminLinkClick}>
                Clic Soporte Admin
            </Button>
        </div>
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

function SuperAdminContent({
  initialSettings,
  isLoading,
  setIsLoading,
  restoreFileInputRef,
}: {
  initialSettings: AppSettings,
  isLoading: boolean,
  setIsLoading: (loading: boolean) => void,
  restoreFileInputRef: React.RefObject<HTMLInputElement>,
}) {
  const form = useFormContext<SettingsFormValues>();
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const [licenseState, setLicenseState] = useState<LicenseState | null>(null);
  const [updateAvailable, setUpdateAvailable] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [isCheckingForUpdate, setIsCheckingForUpdate] = useState(false);

  const handleCheckForUpdate = useCallback(async () => {
    const gitRepoUrl = form.getValues("gitRepositoryUrl");
    if (!gitRepoUrl) {
        toast({ title: "URL no configurada", description: "Por favor, ingrese la URL del repositorio Git primero.", variant: "destructive" });
        return;
    }
    setIsCheckingForUpdate(true);
    try {
        const result = await checkForUpdates(gitRepoUrl, initialSettings.appVersion);
        if (result.updateAvailable) {
            setUpdateAvailable(result.latestVersion);
            toast({ title: "Actualización Disponible", description: `La nueva versión ${result.latestVersion} está lista para instalar.` });
        } else {
            setUpdateAvailable(null);
            toast({ title: "Sistema Actualizado", description: "Ya tiene la última versión del sistema." });
        }
    } catch (error) {
        const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Error desconocido";
        toast({ title: "Error al Comprobar", description: message, variant: "destructive" });
    } finally {
        setIsCheckingForUpdate(false);
    }
  }, [form, toast, initialSettings.appVersion]);

  useEffect(() => {
    getLicenseState().then(setLicenseState);
  }, []);
  
  const generateUpdateScript = () => {
    const repoUrl = form.getValues("gitRepositoryUrl");
    if (!repoUrl) {
        toast({ title: "URL no configurada", description: "Por favor, ingrese y guarde la URL del repositorio Git para generar el script.", variant: "destructive" });
        return;
    }

    const scriptContent = `#!/bin/bash
# Script para actualizar la aplicación Clic Soporte
# Generado automáticamente desde la aplicación

echo "=== Iniciando actualización de Clic Soporte ==="

# Detener el script si un comando falla
set -e

# Opcional: Navega al directorio del proyecto. 
# Si este script no está en la raíz del proyecto, descomente y ajuste la siguiente línea:
# cd /ruta/completa/a/tu/proyecto

echo "1. Obteniendo los últimos cambios desde ${repoUrl}..."
git pull origin main

echo "2. Instalando/actualizando dependencias de Node.js..."
npm install

echo "3. Construyendo la nueva versión de la aplicación Next.js..."
npm run build

echo "4. Recargando la aplicación con PM2 para aplicar cambios sin tiempo de inactividad..."
pm2 reload clic-soporte-cola

echo "======================================================"
echo "¡Aplicación actualizada a la última versión!          "
echo "======================================================"
`;

    const blob = new Blob([scriptContent], { type: 'text/x-shellscript' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = url;
    link.download = `update-app.sh`;
    document.body.appendChild(link);
    link.click();
    document.body.removeChild(link);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    toast({ title: "Script Descargado", description: "El script 'update-app.sh' ha sido descargado." });
  };

  const handleBackup = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const result = await backupDatabase();
      if (result.success && result.data) {
        const blob = new Blob([Buffer.from(result.data, 'base64')], { type: 'application/x-sqlite3' });
        const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        const link = document.createElement('a');
        link.href = url;
        link.download = `clic-soporte-backup-${new Date().toISOString()}.db`;
        document.body.appendChild(link);
        link.click();
        document.body.removeChild(link);
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
        toast({ title: "Copia de Seguridad Descargada", description: "El archivo de la base de datos se ha descargado." });
      } else {
        throw new Error(result.message || 'No se pudo descargar la copia de seguridad.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast({ title: "Error en Copia de Seguridad", description: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Error desconocido.", variant: "destructive" });
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };
  
  const handleRestore = async (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const file = event.target.files?.[0];
    if (!file) return;

    setIsLoading(true);
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = async (e) => {
      try {
        const fileContent = e.target?.result as ArrayBuffer;
        if (!fileContent) throw new Error("No se pudo leer el archivo.");

        const base64Data = Buffer.from(fileContent).toString('base64');
        const result = await restoreDatabase(base64Data);

        if (result.success) {
          toast({ title: "Restauración Exitosa", description: "La base de datos se ha restaurado. La aplicación se recargará." });
          setTimeout(() => window.location.reload(), 2000);
        } else {
          throw new Error(result.message || 'Error en la restauración.');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        toast({ title: "Error en la Restauración", description: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Error desconocido.", variant: "destructive" });
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    };
    reader.onerror = () => {
      toast({ title: "Error de Lectura", description: "No se pudo leer el archivo seleccionado.", variant: "destructive" });
      setIsLoading(false);
    };
    reader.readAsArrayBuffer(file);
    
    if(restoreFileInputRef.current) {
        restoreFileInputRef.current.value = "";
    }
  };

  const handlePurgeData = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
        const result = await purgeHistoricalData();
        if (result.success) {
            toast({ title: "Datos Purgados", description: result.message });
        } else {
            toast({ title: "Error al Purgar", description: result.message, variant: 'destructive' });
        }
    } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

 const handleFactoryReset = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
        const result = await restoreFactorySettings();
        if (result.success) {
            toast({ title: "Restauración Completa", description: result.message });
            setTimeout(() => window.location.reload(), 2000);
        } else {
            toast({ title: "Error en Restauración", description: result.message, variant: 'destructive' });
        }
    } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
    }
 };
  
  return (
    <>
      <div className="border p-4 rounded-lg space-y-3 relative">
          <h4 className="font-semibold flex items-center gap-2"><KeyRound/> Gestión de Licencia</h4>
          <FormField
              control={form.control}
              name="licenseServerDomain"
              render={({ field }) => (
                  <FormItem>
                  <FormLabel>Dominio del Servidor de Licencias</FormLabel>
                  <FormControl><Input placeholder="https://licencias.clicsoporte.com" {...field} /></FormControl>
                  <FormMessage />
                  </FormItem>
              )}
          />
          {licenseState ? (
              <div className='text-sm space-y-1'>
                  <div><strong>Estado: </strong> <Badge variant={licenseState.isValid ? "default" : "destructive"}>{licenseState.status}</Badge></div>
                  <p><strong>Hardware ID: </strong> <span className='font-mono text-xs'>{licenseState.hardwareId}</span></p>
                  <p><strong>Última Sincronización: </strong> {licenseState.lastCheck ? new Date(licenseState.lastCheck).toLocaleString() : 'Nunca'}</p>
              </div>
          ) : <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>Cargando estado de la licencia...</p>}
            <FormField
              control={form.control}
              name="licenseKey"
              render={({ field }) => (
                  <FormItem>
                  <FormLabel>Clave de Licencia Actual</FormLabel>
                  <FormControl><Input placeholder="XXXX-..." {...field} /></FormControl>
                  <FormMessage />
                  </FormItem>
              )}
          />
          <Button onClick={() => activateLicense(form.getValues('licenseKey') || '')} disabled={isLoading} className='w-full' type='button'>
              {isLoading ? <Loader2 className='mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin' /> : <Shield className='mr-2 h-4 w-4'/>}
              Activar o Re-Validar Licencia
          </Button>
      </div>
      
        <div className="border p-4 rounded-lg space-y-3 relative">
          <h4 className="font-semibold flex items-center gap-2"><LifeBuoy /> Sistema de Tickets de Soporte</h4>
          <FormField
              control={form.control}
              name="supportTicketEmbedCode"
              render={({ field }) => (
                  <FormItem>
                  <FormLabel>Código HTML para Incrustar</FormLabel>
                  <FormDesc>Pega aquí el código de inserción (embed) de tu sistema de tickets (ej. osTicket).</FormDesc>
                  <FormControl>
                      <Textarea
                          placeholder='<iframe src="..."&gt;'
                          className="font-mono"
                          rows={6}
                          {...field}
                      />
                  </FormControl>
                  <FormMessage />
                  </FormItem>
              )}
          />
      </div>

      <div className="border p-4 rounded-lg space-y-3 relative">
          <h4 className="font-semibold flex items-center gap-2"><Database/> Copia de Seguridad y Restauración</h4>
          <input type="file" ref={restoreFileInputRef} className="hidden" accept=".db,.sqlite,.sqlite3" onChange={handleRestore} />
          <Button variant="outline" onClick={handleBackup} disabled={isLoading} aria-label="Descargar copia de seguridad" className="w-full" type="button">
              <Download className={`mr-2 h-4 w-4 ${isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
              Descargar Backup
          </Button>
          <AlertDialog>
              <AlertDialogTrigger asChild><Button variant="destructive" className="w-full" disabled={isLoading} type="button"><UploadCloud className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Restaurar desde Backup</Button></AlertDialogTrigger>
              <AlertDialogContent>
              <AlertDialogHeader><AlertDialogTitle>¿Está seguro?</AlertDialogTitle><AlertDialogDescription>Esta acción reemplazará PERMANENTEMENTE la base de datos actual con el archivo que seleccione. Esta acción no se puede deshacer. Se recomienda descargar una copia de seguridad primero.</AlertDialogDescription></AlertDialogHeader>
              <AlertDialogFooter><AlertDialogCancel>Cancelar</AlertDialogCancel><AlertDialogAction onClick={() => restoreFileInputRef.current?.click()} className={cn(buttonVariants({variant: "destructive"}))}>Sí, Restaurar</AlertDialogAction></AlertDialogFooter>
              </AlertDialogContent>
          </AlertDialog>
          <Separator/>
          <AlertDialog>
              <AlertDialogTrigger asChild><Button variant="destructive" className="w-full" disabled={isLoading} type="button"><Factory className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Restaurar Config. de Fábrica</Button></AlertDialogTrigger>
              <AlertDialogContent>
              <AlertDialogHeader><AlertDialogTitle>¿Está absolutamente seguro?</AlertDialogTitle><AlertDialogDescription>Esta acción borrará PERMANENTEMENTE todos los usuarios y configuraciones, y los restaurará a los valores de fábrica. Esta acción no se puede deshacer.</AlertDialogDescription></AlertDialogHeader>
              <AlertDialogFooter><AlertDialogCancel>Cancelar</AlertDialogCancel><AlertDialogAction onClick={handleFactoryReset} className={cn(buttonVariants({variant: "destructive"}))}>Sí, Restaurar Fábrica</AlertDialogAction></AlertDialogFooter>
              </AlertDialogContent>
          </AlertDialog>
      </div>
      
      <Accordion type="single" collapsible className="w-full border rounded-lg">
          <AccordionItem value="update-management">
          <AccordionTrigger className="text-md font-semibold px-4"><div className="flex items-center gap-2"><GitBranchPlus /> Gestión de Actualizaciones</div></AccordionTrigger>
          <AccordionContent className="px-4 pb-4 space-y-4">
                <FormField
                  control={form.control}
                  name="exchangeRateApiUrl"
                  render={({ field }) => (
                      <FormItem>
                      <FormLabel>URL del API para Tipo de Cambio</FormLabel>
                      <FormControl><Input placeholder="http://api.example.com/tdc.json" {...field} /></FormControl>
                      <FormMessage />
                      </FormItem>
                  )}
              />
              <FormField
              control={form.control}
              name="gitRepositoryUrl"
              render={({ field }) => (
                  <FormItem>
                  <FormLabel>URL del Repositorio Git</FormLabel>
                  <FormDesc>URL HTTPS del repositorio para buscar actualizaciones.</FormDesc>
                  <FormControl><Input placeholder="https://github.com/usuario/repo.git" {...field} /></FormControl>
                  <FormMessage />
                  </FormItem>
              )}
              />
              <div className='flex gap-2 items-center'>
                  <Button type="button" onClick={handleCheckForUpdate} variant="outline" disabled={isCheckingForUpdate}>
                      <CloudDownload className={`mr-2 h-4 w-4 ${isCheckingForUpdate ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
                      Buscar Actualizaciones
                  </Button>
                  {updateAvailable && (
                      <Badge variant="default" className="bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700">
                          ¡Versión {updateAvailable} disponible!
                      </Badge>
                  )}
              </div>
              <Separator />
              <div className="space-y-2">
                  <h5 className='font-semibold flex items-center gap-2'><TerminalSquare /> Script de Actualización On-Premise</h5>
                  <Button type="button" variant="outline" onClick={generateUpdateScript} className='w-full'>
                      <Download className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
                      Generar y Descargar Script de Actualización
                  </Button>
              </div>
              <div className="text-xs p-3 rounded-lg bg-muted/50 border space-y-2">
                  <p className='font-bold flex items-center gap-1.5'><Info className='h-4 w-4' />Instrucciones para Actualizar:</p>
                  <ol className="list-decimal list-inside space-y-1">
                      <li>Descargue el script `update-app.sh` con el botón de arriba.</li>
                      <li>Suba el archivo a la carpeta raíz de la aplicación en su servidor.</li>
                      <li>Otorgue permisos de ejecución al script con el comando: `chmod +x update-app.sh`</li>
                      <li>Para actualizar, simplemente ejecute el script desde la terminal: `./update-app.sh`</li>
                      <li>El script se encargará de todo: descargará cambios, instalará dependencias, reconstruirá la app y la reiniciará sin tiempo de inactividad usando PM2.</li>
                  </ol>
              </div>
          </AccordionContent>
          </AccordionItem>
      </Accordion>
      <div className="border p-4 rounded-lg space-y-3 relative text-center">
            <AlertDialog>
              <AlertDialogTrigger asChild><Button variant="destructive" className="w-full" disabled={isLoading} type="button"><Eraser className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Purgar Datos Históricos</Button></AlertDialogTrigger>
              <AlertDialogContent>
              <AlertDialogHeader><AlertDialogTitle>¿Está absolutamente seguro?</AlertDialogTitle><AlertDialogDescription>Esta acción eliminará permanentemente todos los datos de tickets históricos de los reportes. Esta acción no se puede recuperar.</AlertDialogDescription></AlertDialogHeader>
              <AlertDialogFooter><AlertDialogCancel>Cancelar</AlertDialogCancel><AlertDialogAction onClick={handlePurgeData} className={cn(buttonVariants({variant: "destructive"}))}>Sí, Purgar Datos</AlertDialogAction></AlertDialogFooter>
              </AlertDialogContent>
          </AlertDialog>
      </div>
    </>
  );
}

--- File: src/components/settings/UserManagement.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { useForm } from "react-hook-form";
import { zodResolver } from "@hookform/resolvers/zod";
import * as z from "zod";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogDescription,
  DialogFooter,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
  DialogTrigger,
  DialogClose,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import {
  Form,
  FormControl,
  FormField,
  FormItem,
  FormLabel,
  FormMessage,
} from "@/components/ui/form";
import {
    Select,
    SelectContent,
    SelectItem,
    SelectTrigger,
    SelectValue,
} from "@/components/ui/select"
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import { Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow } from "@/components/ui/table";
import { Loader2, PlusCircle, RefreshCw, KeyRound, Edit, Trash2 } from "lucide-react";
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { getUsers, getRoles, createUser, changeUserPassword, updateUser, deleteUser } from "@/actions/userActions";
import type { User, Role, SessionUser } from "@/types/user";
import { Badge } from "../ui/badge";
import { AlertDialog, AlertDialogAction, AlertDialogCancel, AlertDialogContent, AlertDialogDescription, AlertDialogFooter, AlertDialogHeader, AlertDialogTitle, AlertDialogTrigger } from "../ui/alert-dialog";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
import { buttonVariants } from "../ui/button";
import { Checkbox } from "../ui/checkbox";

const createUserSchema = z.object({
  username: z.string().min(3, { message: "El usuario debe tener al menos 3 caracteres." }),
  name: z.string().min(3, { message: "El nombre debe tener al menos 3 caracteres." }),
  password: z.string().min(6, { message: "La contraseña debe tener al menos 6 caracteres." }),
  roleId: z.string({ required_error: "Debe seleccionar un rol." }),
});

type CreateUserFormValues = z.infer<typeof createUserSchema>;

export function UserManagement({ currentUser }: { currentUser: SessionUser | null }) {
  const [users, setUsers] = useState<User[]>([]);
  const [roles, setRoles] = useState<Role[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [isCreateDialogOpen, setIsCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isPasswordDialogOpen, setIsPasswordDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isSubmitting, setIsSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [selectedUser, setSelectedUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
  const [newPassword, setNewPassword] = useState("");
  const [forcePasswordChange, setForcePasswordChange] = useState(false);
  const { toast } = useToast();

  const form = useForm<CreateUserFormValues>({
    resolver: zodResolver(createUserSchema),
    defaultValues: {
      username: "",
      name: "",
      password: "",
      roleId: undefined,
    },
  });

  const fetchUsersAndRoles = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const [usersData, rolesData] = await Promise.all([getUsers(), getRoles()]);
      setUsers(usersData);
      setRoles(rolesData as Role[]);
    } catch (error) {
      toast({
        title: "Error al cargar datos",
        description: "No se pudieron obtener los usuarios y roles.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchUsersAndRoles();
  }, []);

  const onCreateUserSubmit = async (values: CreateUserFormValues) => {
    setIsSubmitting(true);
    const result = await createUser(values.username, values.password, values.name, values.roleId);
    if (result.success) {
      toast({
        title: "Éxito",
        description: result.message,
      });
      setIsCreateDialogOpen(false);
      form.reset();
      await fetchUsersAndRoles(); // Refresh user list
    } else {
      toast({
        title: "Error",
        description: result.message,
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    }
    setIsSubmitting(false);
  };

  const handleChangePassword = async () => {
    if (!selectedUser || !newPassword) return;
    setIsSubmitting(true);
    const result = await changeUserPassword(selectedUser.id, newPassword, forcePasswordChange);
    if (result.success) {
      toast({ title: "Éxito", description: result.message });
      setIsPasswordDialogOpen(false);
      setSelectedUser(null);
      setNewPassword("");
      setForcePasswordChange(false);
    } else {
      toast({ title: "Error", description: result.message, variant: "destructive" });
    }
    setIsSubmitting(false);
  };

   const handleDeleteUser = async (userId: string) => {
    setIsSubmitting(true);
    const result = await deleteUser(userId);
    if (result.success) {
      toast({ title: "Éxito", description: result.message });
      await fetchUsersAndRoles();
    } else {
      toast({ title: "Error", description: result.message, variant: "destructive" });
    }
    setIsSubmitting(false);
  };

  const isAdmin = currentUser?.role === 'admin' || currentUser?.role === 'superadmin';

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                Gestione los usuarios y sus permisos de acceso al sistema.
            </p>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
                 <Dialog open={isCreateDialogOpen} onOpenChange={setIsCreateDialogOpen}>
                    <DialogTrigger asChild>
                        <Button variant="outline"><PlusCircle className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />Crear Usuario</Button>
                    </DialogTrigger>
                    <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-[425px]">
                        <DialogHeader>
                        <DialogTitle>Crear Nuevo Usuario</DialogTitle>
                        <DialogDescription>
                            Complete los campos para añadir un nuevo usuario al sistema.
                        </DialogDescription>
                        </DialogHeader>
                        <Form {...form}>
                            <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onCreateUserSubmit)} className="space-y-4">
                                <FormField
                                    control={form.control}
                                    name="username"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Nombre de usuario</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="puesto01" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                />
                                <FormField
                                    control={form.control}
                                    name="name"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Nombre Completo</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="Jonathan Ugalde" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                />
                                <FormField
                                    control={form.control}
                                    name="password"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Contraseña</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input type="password" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                />
                                <FormField
                                    control={form.control}
                                    name="roleId"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                            <FormLabel>Rol</FormLabel>
                                            <Select onValueChange={field.onChange} defaultValue={field.value}>
                                                <FormControl>
                                                <SelectTrigger>
                                                    <SelectValue placeholder="Seleccione un rol" />
                                                </SelectTrigger>
                                                </FormControl>
                                                <SelectContent>
                                                {roles.map(role => (
                                                    <SelectItem key={role.id} value={role.id}>{role.name}</SelectItem>
                                                ))}
                                                </SelectContent>
                                            </Select>
                                            <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                />
                                 <DialogFooter>
                                    <DialogClose asChild>
                                        <Button type="button" variant="secondary">Cancelar</Button>
                                    </DialogClose>
                                    <Button type="submit" disabled={isSubmitting}>
                                        {isSubmitting && <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />}
                                        Crear Usuario
                                    </Button>
                                </DialogFooter>
                            </form>
                        </Form>
                    </DialogContent>
                </Dialog>
                <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={fetchUsersAndRoles} disabled={isLoading}>
                    <RefreshCw className={`h-4 w-4 ${isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
                </Button>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div className="border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
            <Table>
                <TableHeader>
                <TableRow>
                    <TableHead>Usuario</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Nombre Completo</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Rol</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Estado</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Creado</TableHead>
                    {isAdmin && <TableHead className="text-right">Acciones</TableHead>}
                </TableRow>
                </TableHeader>
                <TableBody>
                {isLoading ? (
                    <TableRow>
                        <TableCell colSpan={isAdmin ? 6 : 5} className="text-center">
                            <Loader2 className="mx-auto h-6 w-6 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
                        </TableCell>
                    </TableRow>
                ) : users.length > 0 ? (
                    users.map((user) => (
                    <TableRow key={user.id}>
                        <TableCell className="font-medium">{user.username}</TableCell>
                        <TableCell>{user.name}</TableCell>
                        <TableCell>{user.roleName}</TableCell>
                        <TableCell>
                            <Badge variant={user.isActive ? 'default' : 'destructive'} className="bg-green-500 hover:bg-green-600">
                                {user.isActive ? "Activo" : "Inactivo"}
                            </Badge>
                        </TableCell>
                        <TableCell>{new Date(user.createdAt).toLocaleDateString()}</TableCell>
                         {isAdmin && (
                            <TableCell className="text-right space-x-1">
                                <Dialog open={isPasswordDialogOpen && selectedUser?.id === user.id} onOpenChange={(isOpen) => { if(!isOpen) { setIsPasswordDialogOpen(false); setForcePasswordChange(false); }}}>
                                    <DialogTrigger asChild>
                                        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={() => { setSelectedUser(user); setIsPasswordDialogOpen(true); }}>
                                            <KeyRound className="h-4 w-4" />
                                        </Button>
                                    </DialogTrigger>
                                    <DialogContent>
                                        <DialogHeader>
                                            <DialogTitle>Cambiar Contraseña para {selectedUser?.username}</DialogTitle>
                                            <DialogDescription>Introduzca la nueva contraseña para el usuario.</DialogDescription>
                                        </DialogHeader>
                                        <div className="space-y-4">
                                            <div className="space-y-2">
                                                <Label htmlFor="newPassword">Nueva Contraseña</Label>
                                                <Input id="newPassword" type="password" value={newPassword} onChange={(e) => setNewPassword(e.target.value)} />
                                            </div>
                                             <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                                                <Checkbox id="forceChange" checked={forcePasswordChange} onCheckedChange={(checked) => setForcePasswordChange(!!checked)} />
                                                <Label htmlFor="forceChange" className="text-sm font-medium leading-none peer-disabled:cursor-not-allowed peer-disabled:opacity-70">
                                                    Forzar cambio en el próximo inicio de sesión
                                                </Label>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <DialogFooter>
                                            <Button variant="ghost" onClick={() => setIsPasswordDialogOpen(false)}>Cancelar</Button>
                                            <Button onClick={handleChangePassword} disabled={isSubmitting || newPassword.length < 6}>
                                                {isSubmitting && <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />}
                                                Guardar Contraseña
                                            </Button>
                                        </DialogFooter>
                                    </DialogContent>
                                </Dialog>
                                <AlertDialog>
                                    <AlertDialogTrigger asChild>
                                      <Button
                                        variant="ghost"
                                        size="icon"
                                        disabled={isSubmitting || currentUser?.id === user.id || (user.roleName === 'Administrador' && currentUser?.role !== 'superadmin') }
                                      >
                                        <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4 text-destructive" />
                                      </Button>
                                    </AlertDialogTrigger>
                                    <AlertDialogContent>
                                      <AlertDialogHeader>
                                        <AlertDialogTitle>¿Está seguro de que desea eliminar a {user.username}?</AlertDialogTitle>
                                        <AlertDialogDescription>
                                          Esta acción es permanente y no se puede deshacer. El usuario será eliminado permanentemente.
                                        </AlertDialogDescription>
                                      </AlertDialogHeader>
                                      <AlertDialogFooter>
                                        <AlertDialogCancel>Cancelar</AlertDialogCancel>
                                        <AlertDialogAction
                                          className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant: "destructive" }))}
                                          onClick={() => handleDeleteUser(user.id)}
                                          disabled={isSubmitting}
                                        >
                                          {isSubmitting ? <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" /> : 'Eliminar'}
                                        </AlertDialogAction>
                                      </AlertDialogFooter>
                                    </AlertDialogContent>
                                  </AlertDialog>
                            </TableCell>
                         )}
                    </TableRow>
                    ))
                ) : (
                    <TableRow>
                        <TableCell colSpan={isAdmin ? 6 : 5} className="text-center text-muted-foreground">
                            No se encontraron usuarios.
                        </TableCell>
                    </TableRow>
                )}
                </TableBody>
            </Table>
        </div>
    </div>
  );
}

--- File: src/components/tools/ToolsClient.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Card, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Accordion, AccordionContent, AccordionItem, AccordionTrigger } from '@/components/ui/accordion';
import { BarChart, Users, Clock, Loader2, RefreshCw, Pencil, UserCog, Settings2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { getAttentionReport, type AttentionReportData } from '@/actions/reportActions';
import { Button } from '../ui/button';
import { useToast } from '@/hooks/use-toast';
import { ToolsQueueConfig } from './ToolsQueueConfig';
import type { AppSettings } from '@/types/settings';
import type { SessionUser } from '@/types/user';
import { UserManagement } from './UserManagement';


export function ToolsClient({ initialSettings, currentUser }: { initialSettings: AppSettings, currentUser: SessionUser }) {
  const [reportData, setReportData] = useState<AttentionReportData[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const { toast } = useToast();

  const fetchReportData = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const data = await getAttentionReport();
      setReportData(data);
    } catch (error) {
      toast({
        title: "Error al Cargar Reporte",
        description: "No se pudieron obtener los datos de atención.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchReportData();
  // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, []);

  const isAdmin = currentUser.role === 'admin' || currentUser.role === 'superadmin';


  return (
    <div className='space-y-6'>
      <Card className="shadow-lg rounded-xl bg-card">
        <CardContent className="p-0">
          <Accordion type="single" collapsible className="w-full" defaultValue="item-1">
            <AccordionItem value="item-1">
              <AccordionTrigger className="text-lg font-semibold px-6">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2"><BarChart /> Reporte de atención por usuario</div>
              </AccordionTrigger>
              <AccordionContent className="px-6 pb-6 space-y-4">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                  <p className="text-muted-foreground">
                    Un resumen de cuántos tiquetes ha atendido cada operador en sus respectivos puestos.
                  </p>
                  <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={fetchReportData} disabled={isLoading}>
                    <RefreshCw className={`h-4 w-4 ${isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : 'mr-2'}`} />
                    {!isLoading && 'Refrescar'}
                  </Button>
                </div>
                <div className="border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
                  <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-border">
                    <thead className="bg-muted/50">
                      <tr>
                        <th scope="col" className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-2"><Users className="h-4 w-4" />Operador</th>
                        <th scope="col" className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider"><Clock className="h-4 w-4 inline mr-1" />Puesto de Trabajo</th>
                        <th scope="col" className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">Tiquetes Atendidos</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody className="bg-card divide-y divide-border">
                      {isLoading ? (
                        <tr>
                          <td colSpan={3} className="text-center py-8">
                            <div className="flex justify-center items-center gap-2 text-muted-foreground">
                              <Loader2 className="h-5 w-5 animate-spin" />
                              Cargando datos...
                            </div>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      ) : reportData.length > 0 ? (
                        reportData.map((row, index) => (
                          <tr key={index}>
                            <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium text-foreground">{row.user}</td>
                            <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-muted-foreground">{row.window}</td>
                            <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-foreground font-bold">{row.count}</td>
                          </tr>
                        ))
                      ) : (
                        <tr>
                          <td colSpan={3} className="text-center py-8 text-muted-foreground">
                            No hay datos de atención para mostrar.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      )}
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
              </AccordionContent>
            </AccordionItem>
            
            <AccordionItem value="item-2">
              <AccordionTrigger className="text-lg font-semibold px-6">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2"><UserCog /> Gestión de Usuarios</div>
              </AccordionTrigger>
              <AccordionContent className="px-6 pb-6 space-y-4">
                  <UserManagement currentUser={currentUser} />
              </AccordionContent>
            </AccordionItem>
            <AccordionItem value="item-3">
               <AccordionTrigger className="text-lg font-semibold px-6">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2"><Settings2 /> Configuración de Cola y Publicidad</div>
              </AccordionTrigger>
              <AccordionContent className="px-6 pb-6">
                <ToolsQueueConfig initialSettings={initialSettings} />
              </AccordionContent>
            </AccordionItem>

          </Accordion>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}

--- File: src/components/tools/ToolsQueueConfig.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState } from 'react';
import { useForm, FormProvider, useFieldArray } from 'react-hook-form';
import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
import * as z from 'zod';
import { Button, buttonVariants } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Form, FormControl, FormField, FormItem, FormLabel, FormMessage, FormDescription as FormDesc } from '@/components/ui/form';
import { Switch } from '@/components/ui/switch';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Textarea } from '@/components/ui/textarea';
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { Save, Loader2, ShoppingCart, Trash2, PlusCircle, HandPlatter, HeartHandshake, Ticket, RefreshCw } from 'lucide-react';
import { Checkbox } from '@/components/ui/checkbox';
import type { AppSettings } from '@/types/settings';
import { updateSettings } from '@/actions/settingsActions';
import { resetQueue } from '@/actions/queueActions';
import { AlertDialog, AlertDialogAction, AlertDialogCancel, AlertDialogContent, AlertDialogDescription, AlertDialogFooter, AlertDialogHeader, AlertDialogTitle, AlertDialogTrigger } from "@/components/ui/alert-dialog";
import { Separator } from '../ui/separator';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

const adCarouselItemSchema = z.object({
  id: z.string().optional(),
  imageUrl: z.string().url({ message: "Por favor, ingrese una URL de imagen válida." }),
  description: z.string().min(5, { message: "La descripción debe tener al menos 5 caracteres." }),
  price: z.string().min(1, { message: "El precio es requerido." }),
});

const queueConfigSchema = z.object({
  isAdFeatureEnabled: z.boolean(),
  adCarouselItems: z.array(adCarouselItemSchema),
  operationMode: z.enum(['single', 'multi']),
  manualDispenserMode: z.boolean(),
  availableWindows: z.array(z.number()),
  preferentialWindows: z.array(z.number()),
  ticketNumberRange: z.object({
      start: z.coerce.number().min(1, "Debe ser mayor a 0."),
      end: z.coerce.number().min(1, "Debe ser mayor a 0."),
  }).refine(data => data.end > data.start, {
      message: "El número final debe ser mayor que el número inicial.",
      path: ["end"],
  }),
  licenseType: z.enum(['free', 'premium']).optional(),
  showExchangeRate: z.boolean(),
});

type QueueConfigFormValues = z.infer<typeof queueConfigSchema>;

export function ToolsQueueConfig({ initialSettings }: { initialSettings: AppSettings }) {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const [isSaving, setIsSaving] = useState(false);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  
  const form = useForm<QueueConfigFormValues>({
    resolver: zodResolver(queueConfigSchema),
    defaultValues: {
      isAdFeatureEnabled: initialSettings.isAdFeatureEnabled ?? false,
      adCarouselItems: initialSettings.adCarouselItems ?? [],
      operationMode: initialSettings.operationMode ?? 'single',
      manualDispenserMode: initialSettings.manualDispenserMode ?? false,
      availableWindows: initialSettings.availableWindows ?? [1],
      preferentialWindows: initialSettings.preferentialWindows ?? [],
      ticketNumberRange: initialSettings.ticketNumberRange ?? { start: 1, end: 999 },
      licenseType: initialSettings.licenseType ?? 'free',
      showExchangeRate: initialSettings.showExchangeRate ?? false,
    },
  });

  const { fields, append, remove } = useFieldArray({
    control: form.control,
    name: "adCarouselItems",
  });

  const onSubmit = async (values: QueueConfigFormValues) => {
    setIsSaving(true);
    try {
        const settingsToUpdate: Partial<AppSettings> = {
            ...values,
            availableWindows: values.operationMode === 'multi' 
                ? Array.from({ length: values.availableWindows.length }, (_, i) => i + 1)
                : [],
        };
        const result = await updateSettings(settingsToUpdate);

      if (result.success) {
        toast({
          title: "Configuración Guardada",
          description: "La configuración de la cola ha sido actualizada.",
        });
        if (result.updatedSettings) {
            form.reset({
              ...result.updatedSettings,
              availableWindows: values.availableWindows,
            });
        }
      } else {
        toast({ title: "Error", description: result.message, variant: "destructive" });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast({ title: "Error de Sistema", variant: "destructive" });
    } finally {
      setIsSaving(false);
    }
  };

  const handleResetQueue = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      await resetQueue();
      toast({ title: "Cola Reiniciada", description: "La cola ha sido reiniciada." });
    } catch (error) {
      toast({ title: "Error de Sistema", variant: "destructive" });
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const watchIsAdFeatureEnabled = form.watch('isAdFeatureEnabled');
  const watchOperationMode = form.watch('operationMode');
  const watchAvailableWindows = form.watch('availableWindows');
  const watchLicenseType = form.watch('licenseType');
  const isFreeLicense = watchLicenseType === 'free';

  return (
    <FormProvider {...form}>
      <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="space-y-6">
        <div className="space-y-4">
            <FormField
                control={form.control} name="operationMode"
                render={({ field }) => (
                <FormItem className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between rounded-lg border p-4">
                    <div className="space-y-0.5"><FormLabel className="text-base">Modo Múltiples Puestos</FormLabel></div>
                    <FormControl><Switch checked={field.value === 'multi'} onCheckedChange={(checked) => {
                        if (isFreeLicense && checked) {
                            toast({ title: "Función Premium", description: "El modo múltiples puestos requiere una licencia de pago.", variant: "destructive"});
                            return;
                        }
                        field.onChange(checked ? 'multi' : 'single');
                    }} disabled={isLoading} /></FormControl>
                </FormItem>
            )}/>
            
            {watchOperationMode === 'multi' && (
            <>
            <FormField
                control={form.control} name="availableWindows"
                render={({ field }) => (
                <div className="space-y-2 border p-4 rounded-lg">
                    <Label>Número de Puestos</Label>
                    <Input type="number" min="1" max="20" defaultValue={field.value.length} onChange={(e) => {
                        const count = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
                        if (!isNaN(count) && count > 0) {
                            if (isFreeLicense && count > 2) {
                                toast({ title: "Límite de Licencia", description: "La licencia gratuita permite un máximo de 2 puestos.", variant: "destructive" });
                                e.target.value = "2";
                                field.onChange(Array.from({length: 2}, (_, i) => i + 1));
                                return;
                            }
                            field.onChange(Array.from({length: count}, (_, i) => i + 1));
                        }
                    }} disabled={isLoading} />
                    <FormDesc>Define cuántos puestos están operativos.</FormDesc>
                </div>
            )}/>
            <FormField
                control={form.control} name="preferentialWindows"
                render={({ field }) => (
                <div className="space-y-2 border p-4 rounded-lg">
                    <Label className='flex items-center gap-2'><HeartHandshake/> Puestos de Atención Preferencial</Label>
                    <FormDesc>Marque los puestos que atenderán tiquetes preferenciales.</FormDesc>
                    <div className='grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 pt-2'>
                        {watchAvailableWindows.map((winNum) => (
                            <FormField
                                key={winNum}
                                control={form.control}
                                name="preferentialWindows"
                                render={({ field: innerField }) => {
                                return (
                                    <FormItem key={winNum} className="flex flex-row items-start space-x-3 space-y-0">
                                    <FormControl>
                                        <Checkbox
                                        checked={innerField.value?.includes(winNum)}
                                        onCheckedChange={(checked) => {
                                            return checked
                                            ? innerField.onChange([...innerField.value, winNum])
                                            : innerField.onChange(innerField.value?.filter((value) => value !== winNum))
                                        }}
                                        />
                                    </FormControl>
                                    <FormLabel className="font-normal">Puesto {winNum}</FormLabel>
                                    </FormItem>
                                )
                                }}
                            />
                        ))}
                    </div>
                </div>
            )}/>
            </>
            )}

            <FormField
                control={form.control} name="manualDispenserMode"
                render={({ field }) => (
                <FormItem className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between rounded-lg border p-4">
                    <div className="space-y-0.5"><FormLabel className="text-base flex items-center gap-2"><HandPlatter/> Modo Dispensador Manual</FormLabel></div>
                    <FormControl><Switch checked={field.value} onCheckedChange={field.onChange} disabled={isLoading} /></FormControl>
                </FormItem>
            )}/>
            
            <div className='space-y-4 border p-4 rounded-lg'>
                <Label className='flex items-center gap-2'><Ticket/> Rango de Tiquetes</Label>
                <div className='flex gap-4'>
                <FormField control={form.control} name="ticketNumberRange.start" render={({ field }) => (
                    <FormItem><FormLabel>Inicio</FormLabel><FormControl><Input type='number' {...field}/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>
                )}/>
                    <FormField control={form.control} name="ticketNumberRange.end" render={({ field }) => (
                    <FormItem><FormLabel>Final</FormLabel><FormControl><Input type='number' {...field}/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>
                )}/>
                </div>
                <FormDesc>La numeración se reiniciará al llegar al final.</FormDesc>
                {form.formState.errors.ticketNumberRange?.end && <FormMessage>{form.formState.errors.ticketNumberRange.end.message}</FormMessage>}
            </div>
        </div>
        <Separator />
        
        {/* Ad Settings */}
        <div className="space-y-4">
            <FormField
            control={form.control}
            name="isAdFeatureEnabled"
            render={({ field }) => (
                <FormItem className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between rounded-lg border p-4">
                <div className="space-y-0.5">
                    <FormLabel className="text-base">Mostrar Carrusel de Publicidad</FormLabel>
                    <FormDesc>Activa para mostrar los anuncios en la pantalla.</FormDesc>
                </div>
                <FormControl><Switch checked={field.value} onCheckedChange={(checked) => {
                    if(isFreeLicense && checked) {
                        toast({title: "Función Premium", description: "La gestión de publicidad requiere una licencia de pago.", variant: "destructive"});
                        return;
                    }
                    field.onChange(checked);
                }} /></FormControl>
                </FormItem>
            )}
            />
             <FormField
                control={form.control}
                name="showExchangeRate"
                render={({ field }) => (
                    <FormItem className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between rounded-lg border p-4">
                    <div className="space-y-0.5">
                        <FormLabel className="text-base">Mostrar Tipo de Cambio (Dólar)</FormLabel>
                    </div>
                    <FormControl><Switch checked={field.value} onCheckedChange={field.onChange} /></FormControl>
                    </FormItem>
                )}
            />
            
            <div className={`space-y-4 ${watchIsAdFeatureEnabled && !isFreeLicense ? 'opacity-100' : 'opacity-50'}`}>
            {fields.map((item, index) => (
                <div key={item.id} className="border p-4 rounded-lg space-y-3 relative">
                <h4 className="font-semibold">Anuncio Cliente #{index + 1}</h4>
                <FormField
                    control={form.control}
                    name={`adCarouselItems.${index}.imageUrl`}
                    render={({ field }) => (
                        <FormItem>
                        <FormLabel>URL de la Imagen</FormLabel>
                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="https://..." {...field} disabled={!watchIsAdFeatureEnabled || isFreeLicense} /></FormControl>
                        <FormMessage />
                        </FormItem>
                    )}
                />
                <FormField
                    control={form.control}
                    name={`adCarouselItems.${index}.description`}
                    render={({ field }) => (
                        <FormItem>
                        <FormLabel>Descripción Corta</FormLabel>
                        <FormControl><Textarea placeholder="Ej: Café de especialidad..." {...field} disabled={!watchIsAdFeatureEnabled || isFreeLicense} rows={2} /></FormControl>
                        <FormMessage />
                        </FormItem>
                    )}
                />
                <FormField
                    control={form.control}
                    name={`adCarouselItems.${index}.price`}
                    render={({ field }) => (
                        <FormItem>
                        <FormLabel>Precio o Texto</FormLabel>
                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="₡10,000" {...field} disabled={!watchIsAdFeatureEnabled || isFreeLicense} /></FormControl>
                        <FormMessage />
                        </FormItem>
                    )}
                />
                <Button type="button" variant="destructive" size="icon" className="absolute top-2 right-2" onClick={() => remove(index)} disabled={!watchIsAdFeatureEnabled || isFreeLicense}>
                    <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                </Button>
                </div>
            ))}
            <Button
                type="button"
                variant="outline"
                className="w-full"
                onClick={() => append({ id: crypto.randomUUID(), imageUrl: 'https://placehold.co/600x400.png', description: '', price: '' })}
                disabled={!watchIsAdFeatureEnabled || isFreeLicense}
            >
                <PlusCircle className="mr-2" /> Agregar Anuncio
            </Button>
            </div>
        </div>
            <Separator />
            <div className='flex gap-4 justify-end'>
            <AlertDialog>
                <AlertDialogTrigger asChild><Button variant="destructive" type="button"><RefreshCw className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Reiniciar Cola</Button></AlertDialogTrigger>
                <AlertDialogContent>
                    <AlertDialogHeader><AlertDialogTitle>¿Está seguro?</AlertDialogTitle><AlertDialogDescription>Esta acción reiniciará los contadores de tickets y limpiará la cola actual.</AlertDialogDescription></AlertDialogHeader>
                    <AlertDialogFooter><AlertDialogCancel>Cancelar</AlertDialogCancel><AlertDialogAction onClick={handleResetQueue} className={cn(buttonVariants({variant: "destructive"}))}>Confirmar</AlertDialogAction></AlertDialogFooter>
                </AlertDialogContent>
            </AlertDialog>
            <Button type="submit" disabled={isSaving}>
                {isSaving ? <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" /> : <Save className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />}
                Guardar Cambios
            </Button>
            </div>
      </form>
    </FormProvider>
  );
}

--- File: src/components/tools/UserManagement.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from "react";
import { useForm } from "react-hook-form";
import { zodResolver } from "@hookform/resolvers/zod";
import * as z from "zod";
import { Button, buttonVariants } from "@/components/ui/button";
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogDescription,
  DialogFooter,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
  DialogTrigger,
  DialogClose,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import {
  Form,
  FormControl,
  FormField,
  FormItem,
  FormLabel,
  FormMessage,
} from "@/components/ui/form";
import {
    Select,
    SelectContent,
    SelectItem,
    SelectTrigger,
    SelectValue,
} from "@/components/ui/select"
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import { Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow } from "@/components/ui/table";
import { Loader2, PlusCircle, RefreshCw, KeyRound, Edit, Trash2, Pencil } from "lucide-react";
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { getUsers, getRoles, createUser, changeUserPassword, updateUser, deleteUser } from "@/actions/userActions";
import type { User, Role, SessionUser } from "@/types/user";
import { Badge } from "../ui/badge";
import { AlertDialog, AlertDialogAction, AlertDialogCancel, AlertDialogContent, AlertDialogDescription, AlertDialogFooter, AlertDialogHeader, AlertDialogTitle, AlertDialogTrigger } from "../ui/alert-dialog";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
import { Checkbox } from "../ui/checkbox";

const createUserSchema = z.object({
  username: z.string().min(3, { message: "El usuario debe tener al menos 3 caracteres." }),
  name: z.string().min(3, { message: "El nombre debe tener al menos 3 caracteres." }),
  password: z.string().min(6, { message: "La contraseña debe tener al menos 6 caracteres." }),
  roleId: z.string({ required_error: "Debe seleccionar un rol." }),
});

type CreateUserFormValues = z.infer<typeof createUserSchema>;

/**
 * A sub-component to allow supervisors to edit user's full names for reporting clarity.
 */
function UserListForSupervisor({ currentUser }: { currentUser: SessionUser }) {
  const [users, setUsers] = useState<User[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [isEditing, setIsEditing] = useState<User | null>(null);
  const [newName, setNewName] = useState("");
  const { toast } = useToast();

  const fetchUsers = useCallback(async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const data = await getUsers();
      setUsers(data);
    } catch (e) {
      toast({ title: "Error", description: "No se pudieron cargar los usuarios.", variant: "destructive" });
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  }, [toast]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchUsers();
  }, [fetchUsers]);

  const handleUpdateName = async () => {
    if (!isEditing) return;
    const result = await updateUser(isEditing.id, newName);
    if (result.success) {
      toast({ title: "Éxito", description: "Nombre actualizado correctamente." });
      setIsEditing(null);
      setNewName("");
      fetchUsers(); // Refresh list
    } else {
      toast({ title: "Error", description: result.message, variant: "destructive" });
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-2">
      <p className="text-muted-foreground">
        Edite el nombre completo de los operadores para una mejor identificación en los reportes.
      </p>
      {isLoading ? (
        <div className="flex justify-center items-center h-24">
          <Loader2 className="h-6 w-6 animate-spin" />
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="border rounded-lg">
          <ul className="divide-y">
            {users.map(user => (
              <li key={user.id} className="p-3 flex justify-between items-center">
                <div>
                  <p className="font-semibold">{user.name || <span className='italic opacity-50'>Sin nombre</span>}</p>
                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">@{user.username} ({user.roleName})</p>
                </div>
                <Dialog open={isEditing?.id === user.id} onOpenChange={(isOpen) => !isOpen && setIsEditing(null)}>
                  <DialogTrigger asChild>
                    <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={() => { setIsEditing(user); setNewName(user.name || ""); }}>
                      <Pencil className="h-4 w-4" />
                    </Button>
                  </DialogTrigger>
                  <DialogContent>
                    <DialogHeader>
                      <DialogTitle>Editar Nombre</DialogTitle>
                      <DialogDescription>
                        Cambie el nombre completo para el usuario @{isEditing?.username}.
                      </DialogDescription>
                    </DialogHeader>
                    <div className="space-y-2">
                      <Label htmlFor="userName">Nombre Completo</Label>
                      <Input id="userName" value={newName} onChange={(e) => setNewName(e.target.value)} />
                    </div>
                    <DialogFooter>
                      <Button variant="ghost" onClick={() => setIsEditing(null)}>Cancelar</Button>
                      <Button onClick={handleUpdateName}>Guardar Cambios</Button>
                    </DialogFooter>
                  </DialogContent>
                </Dialog>
              </li>
            ))}
          </ul>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}


export function UserManagement({ currentUser }: { currentUser: SessionUser | null }) {
  const [users, setUsers] = useState<User[]>([]);
  const [roles, setRoles] = useState<Role[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [isCreateDialogOpen, setIsCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isPasswordDialogOpen, setIsPasswordDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isSubmitting, setIsSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [selectedUser, setSelectedUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
  const [newPassword, setNewPassword] = useState("");
  const [forcePasswordChange, setForcePasswordChange] = useState(false);
  const { toast } = useToast();

  const form = useForm<CreateUserFormValues>({
    resolver: zodResolver(createUserSchema),
    defaultValues: {
      username: "",
      name: "",
      password: "",
      roleId: undefined,
    },
  });
  
  const isAdmin = currentUser?.role === 'admin' || currentUser?.role === 'superadmin';

  const fetchUsersAndRoles = useCallback(async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const [usersData, rolesData] = await Promise.all([getUsers(), getRoles()]);
      setUsers(usersData);
      setRoles(rolesData as Role[]);
    } catch (error) {
      toast({
        title: "Error al cargar datos",
        description: "No se pudieron obtener los usuarios y roles.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  }, [toast]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchUsersAndRoles();
  }, [fetchUsersAndRoles]);
  
  if (!isAdmin) {
      return <UserListForSupervisor currentUser={currentUser!} />
  }

  const onCreateUserSubmit = async (values: CreateUserFormValues) => {
    setIsSubmitting(true);
    const result = await createUser(values.username, values.password, values.name, values.roleId);
    if (result.success) {
      toast({
        title: "Éxito",
        description: result.message,
      });
      setIsCreateDialogOpen(false);
      form.reset();
      await fetchUsersAndRoles(); // Refresh user list
    } else {
      toast({
        title: "Error",
        description: result.message,
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    }
    setIsSubmitting(false);
  };

  const handleChangePassword = async () => {
    if (!selectedUser || !newPassword) return;
    setIsSubmitting(true);
    const result = await changeUserPassword(selectedUser.id, newPassword, forcePasswordChange);
    if (result.success) {
      toast({ title: "Éxito", description: result.message });
      setIsPasswordDialogOpen(false);
      setSelectedUser(null);
      setNewPassword("");
      setForcePasswordChange(false);
    } else {
      toast({ title: "Error", description: result.message, variant: "destructive" });
    }
    setIsSubmitting(false);
  };

   const handleDeleteUser = async (userId: string) => {
    setIsSubmitting(true);
    const result = await deleteUser(userId);
    if (result.success) {
      toast({ title: "Éxito", description: result.message });
      await fetchUsersAndRoles();
    } else {
      toast({ title: "Error", description: result.message, variant: "destructive" });
    }
    setIsSubmitting(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                Gestione los usuarios y sus permisos de acceso al sistema.
            </p>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
                 <Dialog open={isCreateDialogOpen} onOpenChange={setIsCreateDialogOpen}>
                    <DialogTrigger asChild>
                        <Button variant="outline"><PlusCircle className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />Crear Usuario</Button>
                    </DialogTrigger>
                    <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-[425px]">
                        <DialogHeader>
                        <DialogTitle>Crear Nuevo Usuario</DialogTitle>
                        <DialogDescription>
                            Complete los campos para añadir un nuevo usuario al sistema.
                        </DialogDescription>
                        </DialogHeader>
                        <Form {...form}>
                            <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onCreateUserSubmit)} className="space-y-4">
                                <FormField
                                    control={form.control}
                                    name="username"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Nombre de usuario</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="puesto01" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                />
                                <FormField
                                    control={form.control}
                                    name="name"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Nombre Completo</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="Jonathan Ugalde" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                />
                                <FormField
                                    control={form.control}
                                    name="password"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                        <FormLabel>Contraseña</FormLabel>
                                        <FormControl><Input type="password" {...field} /></FormControl>
                                        <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                />
                                <FormField
                                    control={form.control}
                                    name="roleId"
                                    render={({ field }) => (
                                        <FormItem>
                                            <FormLabel>Rol</FormLabel>
                                            <Select onValueChange={field.onChange} defaultValue={field.value}>
                                                <FormControl>
                                                <SelectTrigger>
                                                    <SelectValue placeholder="Seleccione un rol" />
                                                </SelectTrigger>
                                                </FormControl>
                                                <SelectContent>
                                                {roles.map(role => (
                                                    <SelectItem key={role.id} value={role.id}>{role.name}</SelectItem>
                                                ))}
                                                </SelectContent>
                                            </Select>
                                            <FormMessage />
                                        </FormItem>
                                    )}
                                />
                                 <DialogFooter>
                                    <DialogClose asChild>
                                        <Button type="button" variant="secondary">Cancelar</Button>
                                    </DialogClose>
                                    <Button type="submit" disabled={isSubmitting}>
                                        {isSubmitting && <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />}
                                        Crear Usuario
                                    </Button>
                                </DialogFooter>
                            </form>
                        </Form>
                    </DialogContent>
                </Dialog>
                <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={fetchUsersAndRoles} disabled={isLoading}>
                    <RefreshCw className={`h-4 w-4 ${isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
                </Button>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div className="border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
            <Table>
                <TableHeader>
                <TableRow>
                    <TableHead>Usuario</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Nombre Completo</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Rol</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Estado</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Creado</TableHead>
                    {isAdmin && <TableHead className="text-right">Acciones</TableHead>}
                </TableRow>
                </TableHeader>
                <TableBody>
                {isLoading ? (
                    <TableRow>
                        <TableCell colSpan={isAdmin ? 6 : 5} className="text-center">
                            <Loader2 className="mx-auto h-6 w-6 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
                        </TableCell>
                    </TableRow>
                ) : users.length > 0 ? (
                    users.map((user) => (
                    <TableRow key={user.id}>
                        <TableCell className="font-medium">{user.username}</TableCell>
                        <TableCell>{user.name}</TableCell>
                        <TableCell>{user.roleName}</TableCell>
                        <TableCell>
                            <Badge variant={user.isActive ? 'default' : 'destructive'} className="bg-green-500 hover:bg-green-600">
                                {user.isActive ? "Activo" : "Inactivo"}
                            </Badge>
                        </TableCell>
                        <TableCell>{new Date(user.createdAt).toLocaleDateString()}</TableCell>
                         {isAdmin && (
                            <TableCell className="text-right space-x-1">
                                <Dialog open={isPasswordDialogOpen && selectedUser?.id === user.id} onOpenChange={(isOpen) => { if(!isOpen) { setIsPasswordDialogOpen(false); setForcePasswordChange(false); }}}>
                                    <DialogTrigger asChild>
                                        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={() => { setSelectedUser(user); setIsPasswordDialogOpen(true); }}>
                                            <KeyRound className="h-4 w-4" />
                                        </Button>
                                    </DialogTrigger>
                                    <DialogContent>
                                        <DialogHeader>
                                            <DialogTitle>Cambiar Contraseña para {selectedUser?.username}</DialogTitle>
                                            <DialogDescription>Introduzca la nueva contraseña para el usuario.</DialogDescription>
                                        </DialogHeader>
                                        <div className="space-y-4">
                                            <div className="space-y-2">
                                                <Label htmlFor="newPassword">Nueva Contraseña</Label>
                                                <Input id="newPassword" type="password" value={newPassword} onChange={(e) => setNewPassword(e.target.value)} />
                                            </div>
                                             <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                                                <Checkbox id="forceChange" checked={forcePasswordChange} onCheckedChange={(checked) => setForcePasswordChange(!!checked)} />
